```
// ========== HINGLISH PHONETIC SMOOTHING ==========
// Keeps text in Roman script but subtly respells tricky Hinglish words
// so OpenAI TTS pronounces them with natural Indian cadence instead of

function smoothHinglishPhonetics(text: string): string {
  // Only apply to texts that have a mix of English and Hinglish
  // Pure English or pure Devanagari should pass through untouched
  const hasDevanagari = /[\u0900-\u097F]/.test(text);
  const hasHinglish = /\b(hai|nahi|kya|bhai|mera|tera|dost|yaar|pyaar|dil|khushi|maza|sukoon|zindagi|waqt|bilkul|zyada|kam|theek|acha|mast|badiya|haan|ji|bas|aur|lekin|toh|mein|ko|ke|ki|ka|se|ne|tak|jab|tab|ek|do|teen|hai\b|hoga|karega|karunga|lena|dena|aana|jaana|paana|sona|rona|hasna|bolo|karo|chalo|dekho|rukho|jao|aao|mat|nahi|nhi|kyun|kyu|kaise|kaun|kahan|kab|kitna|kaunsa|mera|meri|mere|tera|teri|tere|uska|uski|uske|hamara|hamari|hamare|tumhara|tumhari|tumhare|yeh|woh|yahan|wahan|kisi|koi|kuch|sab|mujhe|tujhe|usse|unse|yeh|woh|subah|sham|raat|din|aaj|kal|abhi|pehle|hamesha|kabhi|zaroor|shayad|bura|buri|bure|acha|achi|ache|accha|bahut|thoda|thodi|thode|sahi|galat|mast|badiya|badhiya|bekar|duniya|zindagi|waqt|sapna|kismat|naseeb|khayal|soch|fikar|himmat|sharam|ghussa|gussa|dar|dua|sach|jhoot|sachai|izzat|beizzati|shukriya|dhanyavaad|namaste|khushi|gham|dard|sukoon|maza|masti|shanti|chain|neend|pyaar|dil|yaar|dost|bhai)\b/i.test(text);

  if (hasDevanagari || !hasHinglish) return text;

  // Word-by-word replacement with case preservation
  return text.replace(/\b([a-zA-Z]+)\b/g, (match) => {
    const lower = match.toLowerCase();
    const replacement = PHONETIC_SMOOTH[lower];
    if (!replacement) return match;
    // Preserve first-letter capitalization
    if (match[0] === match[0].toUpperCase()) {
      return replacement[0].toUpperCase() + replacement.slice(1);
    }
    return replacement;
  });
}
```

import { Logo } from '@/components/Logo';
import type { TypingIndicatorStyle } from '@/hooks/useAppSettings';

interface TypingIndicatorProps {
  style?: TypingIndicatorStyle;
}

export function TypingIndicator({ style = 'dots' }: TypingIndicatorProps) {
  const renderIndicator = () => {
    switch (style) {
      case 'wave':
        return (
          <div className="flex items-end gap-[3px] h-5 pb-0.5">
            {[0, 120, 240].map((d) => (
              <span
                key={d}
                className="inline-block w-[4px] rounded-full bg-violet-400 animate-typing-wave-bar transition-none"
                style={{ animationDelay: `${d}ms`, height: '16px', willChange: 'transform, opacity' }}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        );
      case 'pulse':
        return (
          <div className="flex items-center h-5">
            <span className="inline-block w-4 h-4 rounded-full border-2 border-sky-400 animate-typing-pulse-ring transition-none" style={{ willChange: 'transform, opacity, box-shadow' }} />
          </div>
        );
      case 'orbit':
        return (
          <div className="flex items-center justify-center w-8 h-5">
            <div className="typing-orbit transition-none" style={{ willChange: 'transform' }}>
              <span className="transition-none" style={{ willChange: 'transform' }} /><span className="transition-none" style={{ willChange: 'transform' }} /><span className="transition-none" style={{ willChange: 'transform' }} />
            </div>
          </div>
        );
      case 'neon':
        return (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 h-5">
            {[0, 180, 360].map((d) => (
              <span
                key={d}
                className="inline-block w-[6px] h-[6px] rounded-full bg-cyan-300 animate-typing-neon transition-none"
                style={{ animationDelay: `${d}ms`, willChange: 'transform, opacity, box-shadow' }}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        );
      case 'matrix':
        return (
          <div className="flex items-end gap-[5px] h-5 pb-0.5">
            {[0, 150, 300].map((d) => (
              <span
                key={d}
                className="inline-block w-[5px] rounded-sm bg-emerald-400 animate-typing-matrix transition-none"
                style={{ animationDelay: `${d}ms`, height: '14px', willChange: 'transform, opacity' }}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        );
      case 'fire':
        return (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-[6px] h-5">
            {[0, 120, 240].map((d) => (
              <span
                key={d}
                className="inline-block w-[7px] h-[7px] rounded-[30%] bg-orange-400 animate-typing-fire transition-none"
                style={{ animationDelay: `${d}ms`, willChange: 'transform, opacity' }}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        );
      case 'heart':
        return (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-[6px] h-5">
            {[0, 200, 400].map((d) => (
              <span
                key={d}
                className="inline-block w-[8px] h-[8px] bg-rose-400 animate-typing-heart transition-none"
                style={{ animationDelay: `${d}ms`, willChange: 'transform, opacity' }}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        );
      case 'galaxy':
        return (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-[5px] h-5">
            {[0, 160, 320].map((d) => (
              <span
                key={d}
                className="inline-block w-[7px] h-[7px] rounded-full bg-violet-500 animate-typing-galaxy transition-none"
                style={{ animationDelay: `${d}ms`, willChange: 'transform, opacity' }}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        );
      case 'rocket':
        return (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-[6px] h-5">
            {[0, 150, 300].map((d) => (
              <span
                key={d}
                className="inline-block w-[6px] h-[10px] rounded-sm bg-amber-400 animate-typing-rocket transition-none"
                style={{ animationDelay: `${d}ms`, willChange: 'transform, opacity' }}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        );
      case 'crown':
        return (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-[5px] h-5">
            {[0, 200, 400].map((d) => (
              <span
                key={d}
                className="inline-block w-[8px] h-[8px] rotate-45 bg-yellow-400 animate-typing-crown transition-none"
                style={{ animationDelay: `${d}ms`, willChange: 'transform, opacity' }}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        );
      case 'lightning':
        return (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-[6px] h-5">
            {[0, 120, 240].map((d) => (
              <span
                key={d}
                className="inline-block w-[4px] h-[14px] rounded-sm bg-yellow-300 animate-typing-lightning transition-none"
                style={{ animationDelay: `${d}ms`, willChange: 'transform, opacity' }}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        );
      case 'ocean':
        return (
          <div className="flex items-end gap-[4px] h-5 pb-0.5">
            {[0, 140, 280].map((d) => (
              <span
                key={d}
                className="inline-block w-[6px] rounded-full bg-cyan-400 animate-typing-ocean transition-none"
                style={{ animationDelay: `${d}ms`, height: '14px', willChange: 'transform, opacity' }}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        );
      case 'diamond':
        return (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-[5px] h-5">
            {[0, 180, 360].map((d) => (
              <span
                key={d}
                className="inline-block w-[7px] h-[7px] rotate-45 bg-sky-300 animate-typing-diamond transition-none"
                style={{ animationDelay: `${d}ms`, willChange: 'transform, opacity' }}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        );
      case 'box_up':
        return (
          <div className="flex items-end gap-[4px] h-5 pb-0.5">
            {[0, 120, 240].map((d, i) => (
              <span
                key={d}
                className="inline-block w-[8px] rounded-sm bg-primary animate-typing-box-up transition-none"
                style={{ animationDelay: `${d}ms`, height: i % 2 === 0 ? '10px' : '14px', willChange: 'transform, opacity' }}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        );
      case 'box_down':
        return (
          <div className="flex items-start gap-[4px] h-5 pt-0.5">
            {[0, 120, 240].map((d, i) => (
              <span
                key={d}
                className="inline-block w-[8px] rounded-sm bg-primary animate-typing-box-down transition-none"
                style={{ animationDelay: `${d}ms`, height: i % 2 === 0 ? '14px' : '10px', willChange: 'transform, opacity' }}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        );
      case 'box_bounce':
        return (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-[4px] h-5">
            {[0, 150, 300].map((d) => (
              <span
                key={d}
                className="inline-block w-[8px] h-[8px] rounded-[4px] bg-primary animate-typing-box-bounce transition-none"
                style={{ animationDelay: `${d}ms`, willChange: 'transform, opacity' }}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        );
      // Default dots
      default:
        return (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 h-5">
            {[0, 200, 400].map((d) => (
              <span
                key={d}
                className="inline-block w-[6px] h-[6px] rounded-full bg-primary animate-[typing-pulse_1.4s_ease-in-out_infinite] transition-none"
                style={{ animationDelay: `${d}ms`, willChange: 'transform, opacity' }}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        );
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex gap-3 mb-6 items-start px-2 animate-fade-in">
      <div className="flex-shrink-0 w-8 h-8 rounded-full overflow-hidden bg-primary/10 flex items-center justify-center">
        <Logo size="xs" fit />
      </div>
      <div className="flex flex-col gap-1.5 mt-0.5">
        {renderIndicator()}
        <p className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground/60 font-medium tracking-wide">
          Red Whale is thinking
          <span className="inline-block w-4 text-left animate-pulse">...</span>
        </p>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

// Shared ModeChatPage component - Clean chat interface for all modes
import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
import { Send, Loader2, ArrowLeft } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { toast } from 'sonner';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import type { Message } from '@/types/chat';
import { ChatService } from '@/services/chat';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import ReactMarkdown from 'react-markdown';
import { Logo } from '@/components/Logo';
import { useLanguage } from '@/contexts/LanguageContext';
import { useAppLanguage } from '@/contexts/AppLanguageContext';

interface ModeChatPageProps {
  title: string;
  placeholder?: string;
  emptyTitle?: string;
  emptyDescription?: string;
  examples?: string[];
  sendButtonText?: string;
  systemModeFlags: {
    deepSearch?: boolean;
    proMode?: boolean;
    webSearch?: boolean;
    showThinking?: boolean;
    realTimeMode?: boolean;
    codeMode?: boolean;
    builderMode?: boolean;
    studyMode?: boolean;
    fastMode?: boolean;
    redWhaleMode?: boolean;
    stepByStepMode?: boolean;
    whaleCodeMode?: boolean;
    buildWhaleMode?: boolean;
    howToBuildMode?: boolean;
    planningMode?: boolean;
    timetableMode?: boolean;
    rwIntelligenceMode?: boolean;
    rwV1SuperMode?: boolean;
    webSecretMode?: boolean;
    hackMasterMode?: boolean;
  };
}

export function ModeChatPage({
  title,
  placeholder: placeholderProp = 'Ask anything...',
  emptyTitle,
  emptyDescription,
  examples = [],
  sendButtonText = 'Send',
  systemModeFlags,
}: ModeChatPageProps) {
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Message[]>([]);
  const [input, setInput] = useState('');
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [streamingMessage, setStreamingMessage] = useState('');
  const [abortController, setAbortController] = useState<AbortController | null>(null);
  const scrollRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const inputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);

  const navigate = useNavigate();

  const { t } = useAppLanguage();

  const displayTitle = emptyTitle || title;
  const placeholder = placeholderProp || t('askAnything');

  useEffect(() => {
    if (scrollRef.current) scrollRef.current.scrollTop = scrollRef.current.scrollHeight;
  }, [messages, streamingMessage]);

  useEffect(() => { inputRef.current?.focus(); }, []);

  const handleSend = async () => {
    if (!input.trim() || isLoading) return;
    const userMessage: Message = {
      id: `user_${Date.now()}`,
      role: 'user',

// Logo.tsx - Red Whale Brand Logo
// Premium SVG whale-tail icon. The tail viewed from front naturally forms a "W" shape.
type LogoSize = 'xs' | 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg' | 'xl';

interface LogoProps {
  className?: string;
  size?: LogoSize;
  fit?: boolean;
}

const sizeClassMap: Record<LogoSize, string> = {
  xs: 'w-4 h-4',
  sm: 'w-6 h-6',
  md: 'w-9 h-9',
  lg: 'w-12 h-12',
  xl: 'w-[72px] h-[72px]',
};

const fitClassMap: Record<LogoSize, string> = {
  xs: 'w-3 h-3',
  sm: 'w-4 h-4',
  md: 'w-6 h-6',
  lg: 'w-8 h-8',
  xl: 'w-10 h-10',
};

export function Logo({ className = '', size = 'md', fit = false }: LogoProps) {
  const explicitSize = className.includes('w-') || className.includes('h-');
  const sizeClass = explicitSize ? '' : (fit ? fitClassMap[size] : sizeClassMap[size]);

```
// PDF Generator — Beautiful premium PDFs with Red Whale branding
import { jsPDF } from 'jspdf';
import autoTable from 'jspdf-autotable';

const RED_PRIMARY = '#DC2626';   // red-600
const RED_DARK = '#991B1B';      // red-800
const RED_LIGHT = '#FEE2E2';   // red-100
const TEXT_DARK = '#1F2937';     // gray-800
const TEXT_MUTED = '#6B7280';    // gray-500
const BG_LIGHT = '#FAFAFA';      // gray-50

function stripMarkdown(text: string): string {
  return text
    .replace(/```[\s\S]*?```/g, '')
    .replace(/`([^`]+)`/g, '$1')
    .replace(/\*\*(.+?)\*\*/g, '$1')
    .replace(/\*(.+?)\*/g, '$1')
    .replace(/^#{1,6}\s+/gm, '')
    .replace(/^\s*[•\-\*]\s+/gm, '')
    .replace(/^\s*\d+\.\s+/gm, '')
    .replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\([^)]+\)/g, '$1')
    .replace(/https?:\/\/[^\s\)\]]+/g, '')
    .replace(/\|/g, ' ')
    .replace(/\n{3,}/g, '\n\n')
    .trim();
}

function extractTables(text: string): { before: string; rows: string[][]; after: string }[] {
  const tables: { before: string; rows: string[][]; after: string }[] = [];
  const lines = text.split('\n');
  let i = 0;

  while (i < lines.length) {
    // Look for table header line (contains |)
    if (lines[i].includes('|')) {
      const tableLines: string[] = [];
      let j = i;
      while (j < lines.length && lines[j].includes('|')) {
        tableLines.push(lines[j]);
        j++;
      }
      // Skip separator line (--- or === or :-:)
      if (tableLines.length >= 2) {
        const cleanLines = tableLines.filter(l => !/^\s*[-:|\s]+$/.test(l));
        if (cleanLines.length >= 1) {
          const rows = cleanLines.map(line =>
            line.split('|').map(c => c.trim()).filter(c => c.length > 0)
          ).filter(r => r.length > 0);
          if (rows.length > 0) {
            tables.push({
              before: lines.slice(0, i).join('\n'),
              rows,
              after: lines.slice(j).join('\n'),
            });
            // Continue searching in the after text
            const subTables = extractTables(lines.slice(j).join('\n'));
            tables.push(...subTables);
            return tables;
          }
        }
      }
    }
    i++;
  }
  return tables;
}

function parseStructuredContent(text: string): { type: 'text' | 'table' | 'heading'; content: string; rows?: string[][] }[] {
  const blocks: { type: 'text' | 'table' | 'heading'; content: string; rows?: string[][] }[] = [];
  const lines = text.split('\n');
  let i = 0;

  while (i < lines.length) {
    const line = lines[i];

    // Heading
    const headingMatch = line.match(/^(#{1,6})\s+(.+)/);
    if (headingMatch) {
      blocks.push({ type: 'heading', content: headingMatch[2].trim() });
      i++;
      continue;
    }

    // Table
    if (line.includes('|')) {
      const tableLines: string[] = [];
      let j = i;
      while (j < lines.length && lines[j].includes('|')) {
        tableLines.push(lines[j]);
        j++;
      }
      const cleanLines = tableLines.filter(l => !/^\s*[-:|\s]+$/.test(l));
      const rows = cleanLines.map(l =>
        l.split('|').map(c => c.trim()).filter(c => c.length > 0)
      ).filter(r => r.length > 0);
      if (rows.length > 0) {
        blocks.push({ type: 'table', content: '', rows });
        i = j;
        continue;
      }
    }

    // Regular text (accumulate until next block)
    let textLines: string[] = [];
    while (i < lines.length && !lines[i].match(/^#{1,6}\s+/) && !lines[i].includes('|')) {
      textLines.push(lines[i]);
      i++;
    }
    const content = textLines.join('\n').trim();
    if (content) {
      blocks.push({ type: 'text', content });
    }
  }

  return blocks;
}

export function isStructuredContent(text: string): boolean {
  const hasTable = /\|.+\|/.test(text) && text.split('\n').filter(l => l.includes('|')).length >= 2;
  const hasSchedule = /\b(monday|tuesday|wednesday|thursday|friday|saturday|sunday|time|schedule|timetable|routine|plan|report|summary)\b/i.test(text);
  const hasHeadings = /^#{1,6}\s+/m.test(text);
  const hasLists = /^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/m.test(text);
  return hasTable || (hasSchedule && (hasHeadings || hasLists || hasTable));
}

export async function generatePDF(content: string, title = 'Red Whale Document'): Promise<string> {
  const doc = new jsPDF({
    orientation: 'portrait',
    unit: 'mm',
    format: 'a4',
  });

  const pageWidth = doc.internal.pageSize.getWidth();
  const pageHeight = doc.internal.pageSize.getHeight();
  const margin = 18;
  const contentWidth = pageWidth - margin * 2;

  // ========== HEADER BANNER ==========
  // Red gradient header bar
  doc.setFillColor(220, 38, 38); // red-600
  doc.rect(0, 0, pageWidth, 28, 'F');

  // Subtle darker edge
  doc.setFillColor(153, 27, 27); // red-800
  doc.rect(0, 26, pageWidth, 2, 'F');

  // Red Whale text (left side)
  doc.setTextColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(16);
  doc.text('RED WHALE', margin, 17);

  // Subtitle
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'italic');
  doc.setFontSize(9);
  doc.text('AI-Powered Intelligence', margin, 23);

  // Right side: small icon indicator
  doc.setFillColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setDrawColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.circle(pageWidth - margin - 6, 14, 3, 'S');

  // ========== TITLE ==========
  let y = 40;
  doc.setTextColor(TEXT_DARK);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(18);
  const cleanTitle = stripMarkdown(title).slice(0, 60);
  doc.text(cleanTitle, margin, y);

  // Underline
  doc.setDrawColor(RED_PRIMARY);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.5);
  doc.line(margin, y + 2, margin + doc.getTextWidth(cleanTitle), y + 2);

  y += 12;

  // ========== CONTENT ==========
  const blocks = parseStructuredContent(content);

  for (const block of blocks) {
    // Page break check
    if (y > pageHeight - margin - 15) {
      doc.addPage();
      y = margin;
    }

    if (block.type === 'heading') {
      doc.setTextColor(RED_DARK);
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
      doc.setFontSize(14);
      doc.text(block.content, margin, y);
      y += 8;
    } else if (block.type === 'table' && block.rows && block.rows.length > 0) {
      const headerRow = block.rows[0];
      const bodyRows = block.rows.slice(1);

      autoTable(doc, {
        head: [headerRow],
        body: bodyRows,
        startY: y,
        margin: { left: margin, right: margin },
        theme: 'grid',
        headStyles: {
          fillColor: [220, 38, 38],
          textColor: [255, 255, 255],
          fontStyle: 'bold',
          fontSize: 10,
          halign: 'center',
        },
        bodyStyles: {
          fontSize: 9,
          textColor: [31, 41, 55],
          halign: 'left',
        },
        alternateRowStyles: {
          fillColor: [254, 242, 242],
        },
        styles: {
          font: 'helvetica',
          cellPadding: 3,
          overflow: 'linebreak',
        },
        tableWidth: contentWidth,
      });

      const finalY = (doc as any).lastAutoTable?.finalY || y;
      y = finalY + 8;
    } else if (block.type === 'text') {
      doc.setTextColor(TEXT_DARK);
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
      doc.setFontSize(10);

      const cleanText = stripMarkdown(block.content);
      const splitText = doc.splitTextToSize(cleanText, contentWidth);

      // Page break for long text
      const textHeight = splitText.length * 4.5;
      if (y + textHeight > pageHeight - margin - 10) {
        const availableLines = Math.floor((pageHeight - margin - 10 - y) / 4.5);
        if (availableLines > 2) {
          doc.text(splitText.slice(0, availableLines), margin, y);
        }
        doc.addPage();
        y = margin;
        const remaining = splitText.slice(availableLines);
        doc.text(remaining, margin, y);
        y += remaining.length * 4.5 + 6;
      } else {
        doc.text(splitText, margin, y);
        y += textHeight + 6;
      }
    }
  }

  // ========== FOOTER ==========
  const totalPages = doc.getNumberOfPages();
  for (let p = 1; p <= totalPages; p++) {
    doc.setPage(p);

    // Footer line
    doc.setDrawColor(220, 38, 38);
    doc.setLineWidth(0.3);
    doc.line(margin, pageHeight - 12, pageWidth - margin, pageHeight - 12);

    // Footer text
    doc.setTextColor(TEXT_MUTED);
    doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
    doc.setFontSize(8);
    doc.text('Generated by Red Whale V1', margin, pageHeight - 7);
    doc.text(`Page ${p} of ${totalPages}`, pageWidth - margin - 20, pageHeight - 7);
  }

  return doc.output('datauristring');
}

export function downloadPDF(dataUri: string, filename = 'red-whale-document.pdf'): void {
  const link = document.createElement('a');
  link.href = dataUri;
  link.download = filename;
  link.click();
}
```

```
// DownloadPDFButton — Premium PDF download for structured AI responses
import { useState, useCallback } from 'react';
import { FileDown, Loader2 } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { toast } from 'sonner';
import { generatePDF, downloadPDF, isStructuredContent } from '@/utils/pdfGenerator';

interface DownloadPDFButtonProps {
  content: string;
  title?: string;
}

export function DownloadPDFButton({ content, title = 'Red Whale Document' }: DownloadPDFButtonProps) {
  const [generating, setGenerating] = useState(false);

  const handleDownload = useCallback(async () => {
    if (generating) return;
    setGenerating(true);
    try {
      const dataUri = await generatePDF(content, title);
      const safeTitle = title.replace(/[^a-z0-9\u0900-\u097F\u4e00-\u9fff\uac00-\ud7af]/gi, '-').slice(0, 40);
      downloadPDF(dataUri, `${safeTitle || 'red-whale'}.pdf`);
      toast.success('PDF downloaded!');
    } catch {
      toast.error('Failed to generate PDF. Please try again.');
    }
    setGenerating(false);
  }, [content, title, generating]);

  if (!isStructuredContent(content)) return null;

  return (
    <Button
      variant="ghost"
      size="sm"
      onClick={handleDownload}
      disabled={generating}
      className="h-6 px-2 text-[10px] rounded-full text-primary hover:bg-primary/10"
      title="Download as PDF"
    >
      {generating ? (
        <><Loader2 className="w-3 h-3 mr-1 animate-spin" /> PDF…</>
      ) : (
        <><FileDown className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" /> PDF</>
      )}
    </Button>
  );
}
```

// PDF Generator — Beautiful premium PDFs with Red Whale branding
import { jsPDF } from 'jspdf';
import autoTable from 'jspdf-autotable';

const RED_PRIMARY = '#DC2626';   // red-600
const RED_DARK = '#991B1B';      // red-800
const RED_LIGHT = '#FEE2E2';   // red-100
const TEXT_DARK = '#1F2937';     // gray-800
const TEXT_MUTED = '#6B7280';    // gray-500
const BG_LIGHT = '#FAFAFA';      // gray-50

function stripMarkdown(text: string): string {
  return text
    .replace(/```[\s\S]*?```/g, '')
    .replace(/`([^`]+)`/g, '$1')
    .replace(/\*\*(.+?)\*\*/g, '$1')
    .replace(/\*(.+?)\*/g, '$1')
    .replace(/^#{1,6}\s+/gm, '')
    .replace(/^\s*[•\-\*]\s+/gm, '')
    .replace(/^\s*\d+\.\s+/gm, '')
    .replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\([^)]+\)/g, '$1')
    .replace(/https?:\/\/[^\s\)\]]+/g, '')
    .replace(/\|/g, ' ')
    .replace(/\n{3,}/g, '\n\n')
    .trim();
}

function extractTables(text: string): { before: string; rows: string[][]; after: string }[] {
  const tables: { before: string; rows: string[][]; after: string }[] = [];
  const lines = text.split('\n');
  let i = 0;

  while (i < lines.length) {
    // Look for table header line (contains |)
    if (lines[i].includes('|')) {
      const tableLines: string[] = [];
      let j = i;
      while (j < lines.length && lines[j].includes('|')) {
        tableLines.push(lines[j]);
        j++;
      }
      // Skip separator line (--- or === or :-:)
      if (tableLines.length >= 2) {
        const cleanLines = tableLines.filter(l => !/^\s*[-:|\s]+$/.test(l));
        if (cleanLines.length >= 1) {
          const rows = cleanLines.map(line =>
            line.split('|').map(c => c.trim()).filter(c => c.length > 0)
          ).filter(r => r.length > 0);
          if (rows.length > 0) {
            tables.push({
              before: lines.slice(0, i).join('\n'),
              rows,
              after: lines.slice(j).join('\n'),
            });
            // Continue searching in the after text
            const subTables = extractTables(lines.slice(j).join('\n'));
            tables.push(...subTables);
            return tables;
          }
        }
      }
    }
    i++;
  }
  return tables;
}

function parseStructuredContent(text: string): { type: 'text' | 'table' | 'heading'; content: string; rows?: string[][] }[] {
  const blocks: { type: 'text' | 'table' | 'heading'; content: string; rows?: string[][] }[] = [];
  const lines = text.split('\n');
  let i = 0;

  while (i < lines.length) {
    const line = lines[i];

    // Heading
    const headingMatch = line.match(/^(#{1,6})\s+(.+)/);
    if (headingMatch) {
      blocks.push({ type: 'heading', content: headingMatch[2].trim() });
      i++;
      continue;
    }

    // Table
    if (line.includes('|')) {
      const tableLines: string[] = [];
      let j = i;
      while (j < lines.length && lines[j].includes('|')) {
        tableLines.push(lines[j]);
        j++;
      }
      const cleanLines = tableLines.filter(l => !/^\s*[-:|\s]+$/.test(l));
      const rows = cleanLines.map(l =>
        l.split('|').map(c => c.trim()).filter(c => c.length > 0)
      ).filter(r => r.length > 0);
      if (rows.length > 0) {
        blocks.push({ type: 'table', content: '', rows });
        i = j;
        continue;
      }
    }

    // Regular text (accumulate until next block)
    let textLines: string[] = [];
    while (i < lines.length && !lines[i].match(/^#{1,6}\s+/) && !lines[i].includes('|')) {
      textLines.push(lines[i]);
      i++;
    }
    const content = textLines.join('\n').trim();
    if (content) {
      blocks.push({ type: 'text', content });
    }
  }

  return blocks;
}

export function isStructuredContent(text: string): boolean {
  const hasTable = /\|.+\|/.test(text) && text.split('\n').filter(l => l.includes('|')).length >= 2;
  const hasSchedule = /\b(monday|tuesday|wednesday|thursday|friday|saturday|sunday|time|schedule|timetable|routine|plan|report|summary)\b/i.test(text);
  const hasHeadings = /^#{1,6}\s+/m.test(text);
  const hasLists = /^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/m.test(text);
  return hasTable || (hasSchedule && (hasHeadings || hasLists || hasTable));
}

export async function generatePDF(content: string, title = 'Red Whale Document'): Promise<string> {
  const doc = new jsPDF({
    orientation: 'portrait',
    unit: 'mm',
    format: 'a4',
  });

  const pageWidth = doc.internal.pageSize.getWidth();
  const pageHeight = doc.internal.pageSize.getHeight();
  const margin = 18;
  const contentWidth = pageWidth - margin * 2;

  // ========== HEADER BANNER ==========
  // Red gradient header bar
  doc.setFillColor(220, 38, 38); // red-600
  doc.rect(0, 0, pageWidth, 28, 'F');

  // Subtle darker edge
  doc.setFillColor(153, 27, 27); // red-800
  doc.rect(0, 26, pageWidth, 2, 'F');

  // Red Whale text (left side)
  doc.setTextColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(16);
  doc.text('RED WHALE', margin, 17);

  // Subtitle
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'italic');
  doc.setFontSize(9);
  doc.text('AI-Powered Intelligence', margin, 23);

  // Right side: small icon indicator
  doc.setFillColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setDrawColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.circle(pageWidth - margin - 6, 14, 3, 'S');

  // ========== TITLE ==========
  let y = 40;
  doc.setTextColor(TEXT_DARK);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(18);
  const cleanTitle = stripMarkdown(title).slice(0, 60);
  doc.text(cleanTitle, margin, y);

  // Underline
  doc.setDrawColor(RED_PRIMARY);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.5);
  doc.line(margin, y + 2, margin + doc.getTextWidth(cleanTitle), y + 2);

  y += 12;

  // ========== CONTENT ==========
  const blocks = parseStructuredContent(content);

  for (const block of blocks) {
    // Page break check
    if (y > pageHeight - margin - 15) {
      doc.addPage();
      y = margin;
    }

    if (block.type === 'heading') {
      doc.setTextColor(RED_DARK);
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
      doc.setFontSize(14);
      doc.text(block.content, margin, y);
      y += 8;
    } else if (block.type === 'table' && block.rows && block.rows.length > 0) {
      const headerRow = block.rows[0];
      const bodyRows = block.rows.slice(1);

      autoTable(doc, {
        head: [headerRow],
        body: bodyRows,
        startY: y,
        margin: { left: margin, right: margin },
        theme: 'grid',
        headStyles: {
          fillColor: [220, 38, 38],
          textColor: [255, 255, 255],
          fontStyle: 'bold',
          fontSize: 10,
          halign: 'center',
        },
        bodyStyles: {
          fontSize: 9,
          textColor: [31, 41, 55],
          halign: 'left',
        },
        alternateRowStyles: {
          fillColor: [254, 242, 242],
        },
        styles: {
          font: 'helvetica',
          cellPadding: 3,
          overflow: 'linebreak',
        },
        tableWidth: contentWidth,
      });

      const finalY = (doc as any).lastAutoTable?.finalY || y;
      y = finalY + 8;
    } else if (block.type === 'text') {
      doc.setTextColor(TEXT_DARK);
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
      doc.setFontSize(10);

      const cleanText = stripMarkdown(block.content);
      const splitText = doc.splitTextToSize(cleanText, contentWidth);

      // Page break for long text
      const textHeight = splitText.length * 4.5;
      if (y + textHeight > pageHeight - margin - 10) {
        const availableLines = Math.floor((pageHeight - margin - 10 - y) / 4.5);
        if (availableLines > 2) {
          doc.text(splitText.slice(0, availableLines), margin, y);
        }
        doc.addPage();
        y = margin;
        const remaining = splitText.slice(availableLines);
        doc.text(remaining, margin, y);
        y += remaining.length * 4.5 + 6;
      } else {
        doc.text(splitText, margin, y);
        y += textHeight + 6;
      }
    }
  }

  // ========== FOOTER ==========
  const totalPages = doc.getNumberOfPages();
  for (let p = 1; p <= totalPages; p++) {
    doc.setPage(p);

    // Footer line
    doc.setDrawColor(220, 38, 38);
    doc.setLineWidth(0.3);
    doc.line(margin, pageHeight - 12, pageWidth - margin, pageHeight - 12);

    // Footer text
    doc.setTextColor(TEXT_MUTED);
    doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
    doc.setFontSize(8);
    doc.text('Generated by Red Whale V1', margin, pageHeight - 7);
    doc.text(`Page ${p} of ${totalPages}`, pageWidth - margin - 20, pageHeight - 7);
  }

  return doc.output('datauristring');
}

export function downloadPDF(dataUri: string, filename = 'red-whale-document.pdf'): void {
  const link = document.createElement('a');
  link.href = dataUri;
  link.download = filename;
  link.click();
}

```
// PDF Generator — Beautiful premium PDFs with Red Whale branding
import { jsPDF } from 'jspdf';
import autoTable from 'jspdf-autotable';

const RED_PRIMARY = '#DC2626';   // red-600
const RED_DARK = '#991B1B';      // red-800
const RED_LIGHT = '#FEE2E2';   // red-100
const TEXT_DARK = '#1F2937';     // gray-800
const TEXT_MUTED = '#6B7280';    // gray-500

function stripMarkdown(text: string): string {
  return text
    .replace(/```[\s\S]*?```/g, '')
    .replace(/`([^`]+)`/g, '$1')
    .replace(/\*\*(.+?)\*\*/g, '$1')
    .replace(/\*(.+?)\*/g, '$1')
    .replace(/^#{1,6}\s+/gm, '')
    .replace(/^\s*[•\-\*]\s+/gm, '')
    .replace(/^\s*\d+\.\s+/gm, '')
    .replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\([^)]+\)/g, '$1')
    .replace(/https?:\/\/[^\s\)\]]+/g, '')
    .replace(/\|/g, ' ')
    .replace(/\n{3,}/g, '\n\n')
    .trim();
}

function extractTables(text: string): { before: string; rows: string[][]; after: string }[] {
  const tables: { before: string; rows: string[][]; after: string }[] = [];
  const lines = text.split('\n');
  let i = 0;

  while (i < lines.length) {
    // Look for table header line (contains |)
    if (lines[i].includes('|')) {
      const tableLines: string[] = [];
      let j = i;
      while (j < lines.length && lines[j].includes('|')) {
        tableLines.push(lines[j]);
        j++;
      }
      // Skip separator line (--- or === or :-:)
      if (tableLines.length >= 2) {
        const cleanLines = tableLines.filter(l => !/^\s*[-:|\s]+$/.test(l));
        if (cleanLines.length >= 1) {
          const rows = cleanLines.map(line =>
            line.split('|').map(c => c.trim()).filter(c => c.length > 0)
          ).filter(r => r.length > 0);
          if (rows.length > 0) {
            tables.push({
              before: lines.slice(0, i).join('\n'),
              rows,
              after: lines.slice(j).join('\n'),
            });
            // Continue searching in the after text
            const subTables = extractTables(lines.slice(j).join('\n'));
            tables.push(...subTables);
            return tables;
          }
        }
      }
    }
    i++;
  }
  return tables;
}

function parseStructuredContent(text: string): { type: 'text' | 'table' | 'heading'; content: string; rows?: string[][] }[] {
  const blocks: { type: 'text' | 'table' | 'heading'; content: string; rows?: string[][] }[] = [];
  const lines = text.split('\n');
  let i = 0;

  while (i < lines.length) {
    const line = lines[i];

    // Heading
    const headingMatch = line.match(/^(#{1,6})\s+(.+)/);
    if (headingMatch) {
      blocks.push({ type: 'heading', content: headingMatch[2].trim() });
      i++;
      continue;
    }

    // Table
    if (line.includes('|')) {
      const tableLines: string[] = [];
      let j = i;
      while (j < lines.length && lines[j].includes('|')) {
        tableLines.push(lines[j]);
        j++;
      }
      const cleanLines = tableLines.filter(l => !/^\s*[-:|\s]+$/.test(l));
      const rows = cleanLines.map(l =>
        l.split('|').map(c => c.trim()).filter(c => c.length > 0)
      ).filter(r => r.length > 0);
      if (rows.length > 0) {
        blocks.push({ type: 'table', content: '', rows });
        i = j;
        continue;
      }
    }

    // Regular text (accumulate until next block)
    let textLines: string[] = [];
    while (i < lines.length && !lines[i].match(/^#{1,6}\s+/) && !lines[i].includes('|')) {
      textLines.push(lines[i]);
      i++;
    }
    const content = textLines.join('\n').trim();
    if (content) {
      blocks.push({ type: 'text', content });
    }
  }

  return blocks;
}

export function isStructuredContent(text: string): boolean {
  const hasTable = /\|.+\|/.test(text) && text.split('\n').filter(l => l.includes('|')).length >= 2;
  const hasSchedule = /\b(monday|tuesday|wednesday|thursday|friday|saturday|sunday|time|schedule|timetable|routine|plan|report|summary)\b/i.test(text);
  const hasHeadings = /^#{1,6}\s+/m.test(text);
  const hasLists = /^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/m.test(text);
  return hasTable || (hasSchedule && (hasHeadings || hasLists || hasTable));
}
```

```
// PDF Generator — Clean premium PDFs with Red Whale branding
import { jsPDF } from 'jspdf';

const RED_PRIMARY = '#DC2626';
const RED_DARK = '#991B1B';
const TEXT_DARK = '#1F2937';
const TEXT_MUTED = '#6B7280';

function toPlainText(text: string): string {
  return text
    // Remove code blocks entirely
    .replace(/```[\s\S]*?```/g, '')
    // Remove inline code backticks
    .replace(/`([^`]*)`/g, '$1')
    // Remove bold/italic markdown
    .replace(/\*\*([^*]+)\*\*/g, '$1')
    .replace(/\*([^*]+)\*/g, '$1')
    .replace(/__([^_]+)__/g, '$1')
    .replace(/_([^_]+)_/g, '$1')
    // Remove heading markers, keep the text
    .replace(/^#{1,6}\s+/gm, '')
    // Remove bullet/list markers
    .replace(/^\s*[•\-\*]\s+/gm, '')
    .replace(/^\s*\d+\.\s+/gm, '')
    // Remove links — keep link text only
    .replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\([^)]+\)/g, '$1')
    .replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\[[^\]]*\]/g, '$1')
    // Remove bare URLs
    .replace(/https?:\/\/[^\s]+/g, '')
    // Remove table pipes and separators
    .replace(/\|/g, '')
    // Remove leftover table separator lines
    .replace(/^\s*[-:]+[-\s:]*\s*$/gm, '')
    // Clean up extra whitespace
    .replace(/[ \t]+/g, ' ')
    .replace(/\n{3,}/g, '\n\n')
    .trim();
}

export function isStructuredContent(text: string): boolean {
  const hasTable = /\|.+/m.test(text);
  const hasSchedule = /\b(monday|tuesday|wednesday|thursday|friday|saturday|sunday|time|schedule|timetable|routine|plan|report|summary|table|chart|list)\b/i.test(text);
  const hasHeadings = /^#{1,6}\s+/m.test(text);
  const hasLists = /^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/m.test(text);
  return hasTable || (hasSchedule && (hasHeadings || hasLists));
}

export async function generatePDF(content: string, title = 'Red Whale Document'): Promise<string> {
  const doc = new jsPDF({
    orientation: 'portrait',
    unit: 'mm',
    format: 'a4',
  });

  const pageWidth = doc.internal.pageSize.getWidth();
  const pageHeight = doc.internal.pageSize.getHeight();
  const margin = 18;
  const contentWidth = pageWidth - margin * 2;

  // ===== HEADER =====
  doc.setFillColor(220, 38, 38);
  doc.rect(0, 0, pageWidth, 26, 'F');
  doc.setFillColor(153, 27, 27);
  doc.rect(0, 24, pageWidth, 2, 'F');

  doc.setTextColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(16);
  doc.text('RED WHALE', margin, 16);

  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'italic');
  doc.setFontSize(9);
  doc.text('AI-Powered Intelligence', margin, 22);

  // ===== TITLE =====
  let y = 38;
  const cleanTitle = toPlainText(title).slice(0, 60);
  doc.setTextColor(TEXT_DARK);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(16);
  doc.text(cleanTitle, margin, y);

  doc.setDrawColor(RED_PRIMARY);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.5);
  doc.line(margin, y + 2, margin + doc.getTextWidth(cleanTitle), y + 2);

  y += 12;

  // ===== CONTENT =====
  const plain = toPlainText(content);
  const lines = plain.split('\n');
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
  doc.setFontSize(10);
  doc.setTextColor(TEXT_DARK);

  for (const rawLine of lines) {
    const line = rawLine.trim();
    if (!line) {
      y += 4;
      continue;
    }

    // Detect headings by uppercase or short bold-looking lines
    const isHeading = line.length < 50 && /^[A-Z0-9][A-Z0-9\s\-:]{3,}$/i.test(line) && line.split(' ').length <= 6;

    if (isHeading) {
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
      doc.setFontSize(12);
      doc.setTextColor(RED_DARK);
    } else {
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
      doc.setFontSize(10);
      doc.setTextColor(TEXT_DARK);
    }

    const split = doc.splitTextToSize(line, contentWidth);
    const lineHeight = isHeading ? 5 : 4.5;

    // Page break
    if (y + split.length * lineHeight > pageHeight - margin - 12) {
      doc.addPage();
      y = margin;
    }

    doc.text(split, margin, y);
    y += split.length * lineHeight + (isHeading ? 3 : 2);
  }

  // ===== FOOTER =====
  const totalPages = doc.getNumberOfPages();
  for (let p = 1; p <= totalPages; p++) {
    doc.setPage(p);
    doc.setDrawColor(220, 38, 38);
    doc.setLineWidth(0.3);
    doc.line(margin, pageHeight - 12, pageWidth - margin, pageHeight - 12);

    doc.setTextColor(TEXT_MUTED);
    doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
    doc.setFontSize(8);
    doc.text('Generated by Red Whale V1', margin, pageHeight - 7);
    doc.text(`Page ${p} of ${totalPages}`, pageWidth - margin - 20, pageHeight - 7);
  }

  return doc.output('datauristring');
}

export function downloadPDF(dataUri: string, filename = 'red-whale-document.pdf'): void {
  const link = document.createElement('a');
  link.href = dataUri;
  link.download = filename;
  link.click();
}
```

Room Temperature Rules: Ensure your butter, eggs, and milk are all at room temperature. This allows them to
emulsify properly, creating a smoother batter and a more uniform cake texture. Cold ingredients can cause the
batter to curdle.
Avoid Overmixing: This is the cardinal rule of cake baking. Overmixing develops the gluten in the flour, making
your cake tough, dense, and dry instead of light and airy. Mix only until just combined.
Weigh Your Flour: For professional-level precision, always weigh your flour using a kitchen scale rather than
measuring by volume. A cup of flour can vary significantly depending on how it's packed, leading to inconsistent
results.
Oven Thermometer: Invest in an inexpensive oven thermometer. Most built-in oven thermostats are inaccurate
by 10-20°C, which can sabotage your baking efforts. An external thermometer ensures you're baking at the
exact temperature required.

```
// PDF Generator — Clean premium PDFs with Red Whale branding
import { jsPDF } from 'jspdf';

const RED_PRIMARY = '#DC2626';
const RED_DARK = '#991B1B';
const TEXT_DARK = '#1F2937';
const TEXT_MUTED = '#6B7280';

function toPlainText(text: string): string {
  return text
    // Remove code blocks entirely
    .replace(/```[\s\S]*?```/g, '')
    // Remove inline code backticks
    .replace(/`([^`]*)`/g, '$1')
    // Remove bold/italic markdown
    .replace(/\*\*([^*]+)\*\*/g, '$1')
    .replace(/\*([^*]+)\*/g, '$1')
    .replace(/__([^_]+)__/g, '$1')
    .replace(/_([^_]+)_/g, '$1')
    // Remove heading markers, keep the text
    .replace(/^#{1,6}\s+/gm, '')
    // Remove bullet/list markers
    .replace(/^\s*[•\-\*]\s+/gm, '')
    .replace(/^\s*\d+\.\s+/gm, '')
    // Remove links — keep link text only
    .replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\([^)]+\)/g, '$1')
    .replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\[[^\]]*\]/g, '$1')
    // Remove bare URLs
    .replace(/https?:\/\/[^\s]+/g, '')
    // Remove table pipes and separators
    .replace(/\|/g, '')
    // Remove leftover table separator lines
    .replace(/^\s*[-:]+[-\s:]*\s*$/gm, '')
    // Clean up extra whitespace
    .replace(/[ \t]+/g, ' ')
    .replace(/\n{3,}/g, '\n\n')
    .trim();
}

export function isStructuredContent(text: string): boolean {
  const hasTable = /\|.+/m.test(text);
  const hasSchedule = /\b(monday|tuesday|wednesday|thursday|friday|saturday|sunday|time|schedule|timetable|routine|plan|report|summary|table|chart|list)\b/i.test(text);
  const hasHeadings = /^#{1,6}\s+/m.test(text);
  const hasLists = /^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/m.test(text);
  return hasTable || (hasSchedule && (hasHeadings || hasLists));
}

export async function generatePDF(content: string, title = 'Red Whale Document'): Promise<string> {
  const doc = new jsPDF({
    orientation: 'portrait',
    unit: 'mm',
    format: 'a4',
  });

  const pageWidth = doc.internal.pageSize.getWidth();
  const pageHeight = doc.internal.pageSize.getHeight();
  const margin = 18;
  const contentWidth = pageWidth - margin * 2;

  // ===== HEADER =====
  doc.setFillColor(220, 38, 38);
  doc.rect(0, 0, pageWidth, 26, 'F');
  doc.setFillColor(153, 27, 27);
  doc.rect(0, 24, pageWidth, 2, 'F');

  doc.setTextColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(16);
  doc.text('RED WHALE', margin, 16);

  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'italic');
  doc.setFontSize(9);
  doc.text('AI-Powered Intelligence', margin, 22);

  // ===== TITLE =====
  let y = 38;
  const cleanTitle = toPlainText(title).slice(0, 60);
  doc.setTextColor(TEXT_DARK);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(16);
  doc.text(cleanTitle, margin, y);

  doc.setDrawColor(RED_PRIMARY);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.5);
  doc.line(margin, y + 2, margin + doc.getTextWidth(cleanTitle), y + 2);

  y += 12;

  // ===== CONTENT =====
  const plain = toPlainText(content);
  const lines = plain.split('\n');
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
  doc.setFontSize(10);
  doc.setTextColor(TEXT_DARK);

  for (const rawLine of lines) {
    const line = rawLine.trim();
    if (!line) {
      y += 4;
      continue;
    }

    // Detect headings by uppercase or short bold-looking lines
    const isHeading = line.length < 50 && /^[A-Z0-9][A-Z0-9\s\-:]{3,}$/i.test(line) && line.split(' ').length <= 6;

    if (isHeading) {
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
      doc.setFontSize(12);
      doc.setTextColor(RED_DARK);
    } else {
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
      doc.setFontSize(10);
      doc.setTextColor(TEXT_DARK);
    }

    const split = doc.splitTextToSize(line, contentWidth);
    const lineHeight = isHeading ? 5 : 4.5;

    // Page break
    if (y + split.length * lineHeight > pageHeight - margin - 12) {
      doc.addPage();
      y = margin;
    }

    doc.text(split, margin, y);
    y += split.length * lineHeight + (isHeading ? 3 : 2);
  }

  // ===== FOOTER =====
  const totalPages = doc.getNumberOfPages();
  for (let p = 1; p <= totalPages; p++) {
    doc.setPage(p);
    doc.setDrawColor(220, 38, 38);
    doc.setLineWidth(0.3);
    doc.line(margin, pageHeight - 12, pageWidth - margin, pageHeight - 12);

    doc.setTextColor(TEXT_MUTED);
    doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
    doc.setFontSize(8);
    doc.text('Generated by Red Whale V1', margin, pageHeight - 7);
    doc.text(`Page ${p} of ${totalPages}`, pageWidth - margin - 20, pageHeight - 7);
  }

  return doc.output('datauristring');
}

export function downloadPDF(dataUri: string, filename = 'red-whale-document.pdf'): void {
  const link = document.createElement('a');
  link.href = dataUri;
  link.download = filename;
  link.click();
}
```

New String: ```
// PDF Generator — Premium beautiful PDFs with Red Whale branding
import { jsPDF } from 'jspdf';

/* ─── helpers ─── */

// Strip all formatting, markdown, and weird unicode artifacts
function cleanText(text: string): string {
  return (
    text
      // code blocks
      .replace(/```[\s\S]*?```/g, '')
      // inline code
      .replace(/`([^`]*)`/g, '$1')
      // bold / italic / underline markdown
      .replace(/\*\*([^*]+)\*\*/g, '$1')
      .replace(/\*([^*]+)\*/g, '$1')
      .replace(/__([^_]+)__/g, '$1')
      .replace(/_([^_]+)_/g, '$1')
      // heading hashes
      .replace(/^#{1,6}\s+/gm, '')
      // bullet / list markers
      .replace(/^\s*[•\-\*]\s+/gm, '')
      .replace(/^\s*\d+\.\s+/gm, '')
      // markdown links → just text
      .replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\([^)]+\)/g, '$1')
      .replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\[[^\]]*\]/g, '$1')
      // bare URLs
      .replace(/https?:\/\/[^\s]+/g, '')
      // table pipes & separator lines
      .replace(/\|/g, '')
      .replace(/^\s*[-:]+[-\s:]*\s*$/gm, '')
      // Remove ALL private-use / control / combining / unusual Unicode
      // Keep: Basic Latin, Latin-1, Devanagari, CJK, common symbols
      .replace(/[\uE000-\uF8FF]/g, '')   // Private Use Area
      .replace(/[\uFFF0-\uFFFF]/g, '')   // Specials
      .replace(/[\u0080-\u009F]/g, '')   // C1 controls
      .replace(/[\u0600-\u06FF]/g, '')   // Arabic
      .replace(/[\u0E00-\u0E7F]/g, '')   // Thai
      .replace(/[\u0370-\u03FF]/g, '')   // Greek
      .replace(/[\u0400-\u04FF]/g, '')   // Cyrillic
      .replace(/[\u0100-\u017F]/g, '')   // Latin Extended-A
      .replace(/[\u0180-\u024F]/g, '')   // Latin Extended-B
      .replace(/[\u0300-\u036F]/g, '')   // Combining diacritical marks
      // Remove weird letter-by-letter spaced words (e.g. "M U S T :"  or "c a k e")
      .replace(/\b([A-Za-z])\s(?=\s*[A-Za-z]\b)/g, '')
      .replace(/\b([A-Za-z]) (?=[A-Za-z]\b)/g, '')
      // Clean extra whitespace
      .replace(/[ \t]+/g, ' ')
      .replace(/\n{3,}/g, '\n\n')
      .trim()
  );
}

function getDateStr(): string {
  const d = new Date();
  return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
    year: 'numeric',
    month: 'long',
    day: 'numeric',
  });
}

/* ─── detect whether a PDF button should show ─── */
export function isStructuredContent(text: string): boolean {
  const hasTable = /\|.+/m.test(text);
  const hasSchedule = /\b(monday|tuesday|wednesday|thursday|friday|saturday|sunday|time|schedule|timetable|routine|plan|report|summary|table|chart|list|ingredient|step|material)\b/i.test(text);
  const hasHeadings = /^#{1,6}\s+/m.test(text);
  const hasLists = /^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/m.test(text);
  return hasTable || (hasSchedule && (hasHeadings || hasLists));
}

/* ─── main PDF builder ─── */
export async function generatePDF(rawContent: string, title = 'Red Whale Document'): Promise<string> {
  const doc = new jsPDF({ orientation: 'portrait', unit: 'mm', format: 'a4' });

  const PW = doc.internal.pageSize.getWidth();   // 210
  const PH = doc.internal.pageSize.getHeight();  // 297
  const M = 20;                                    // margin
  const CW = PW - M * 2;                           // content width

  const content = cleanText(rawContent);
  const docTitle = cleanText(title).slice(0, 60);

  /* ═══════ PAGE 1 — COVER ═══════ */
  // Red top banner
  doc.setFillColor(185, 28, 28); // red-700
  doc.rect(0, 0, PW, 55, 'F');

  // Subtle bottom edge of banner
  doc.setFillColor(127, 29, 29); // red-900
  doc.rect(0, 53, PW, 2, 'F');

  // "RED WHALE" on cover
  doc.setTextColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(28);
  doc.text('RED WHALE', M, 28);

  // Subtitle
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'italic');
  doc.setFontSize(11);
  doc.text('AI-Powered Intelligence', M, 37);

  // Decorative circle on right side of banner
  doc.setDrawColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.8);
  doc.circle(PW - M - 12, 30, 8, 'S');
  doc.circle(PW - M - 12, 30, 4, 'S');

  // Document title (below banner)
  let y = 70;
  doc.setTextColor(31, 41, 55);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(20);
  const titleLines = doc.splitTextToSize(docTitle, CW);
  doc.text(titleLines, M, y);
  y += titleLines.length * 8 + 2;

  // Red accent line under title
  doc.setDrawColor(185, 28, 28);
  doc.setLineWidth(1);
  const tw = doc.getTextWidth(docTitle);
  doc.line(M, y, M + Math.min(tw, CW), y);
  y += 10;

  // Date
  doc.setTextColor(107, 114, 128);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
  doc.setFontSize(10);
  doc.text(getDateStr(), M, y);
  y += 14;

  // Horizontal divider
  doc.setDrawColor(200, 200, 200);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.2);
  doc.line(M, y, PW - M, y);
  y += 10;

  /* ═══════ CONTENT PAGES ═══════ */
  const bodyLines = content.split('\n');
  const RED = [185, 28, 28];
  const DARK = [31, 41, 55];
  const MUTED = [107, 114, 128];

  for (const raw of bodyLines) {
    const line = raw.trim();
    if (!line) {
      y += 4;
      continue;
    }

    // ── Detect section headings ──
    // Heuristic: short (<55 chars), ≤6 words, no lowercase starting words
    const words = line.split(/\s+/);
    const looksLikeHeading =
      line.length < 55 &&
      words.length <= 8 &&
      /^[A-Z0-9]/.test(line) &&
      !/\b(and|the|for|with|from|into|onto|upon|this|that|these|those|when|where|because|since|while|during|before|after|above|below|between|under|over|again|further|then|once|here|there|all|any|both|each|few|more|most|other|some|such|no|nor|not|only|own|same|so|than|too|very|can|will|just|should|now)\b/i.test(words[0] || '');

    // Page break
    const lineH = looksLikeHeading ? 5.5 : 4.8;
    const needed = looksLikeHeading ? 14 : 6;
    if (y + needed > PH - M - 10) {
      doc.addPage();
      y = M;
    }

    if (looksLikeHeading) {
      // Small red square bullet
      doc.setFillColor(...RED);
      doc.rect(M, y - 2.5, 3, 3, 'F');

      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
      doc.setFontSize(12);
      doc.setTextColor(...RED);
      doc.text(line, M + 5, y);
      y += 10;
    } else {
      // Body text
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
      doc.setFontSize(10);
      doc.setTextColor(...DARK);

      const wrapped = doc.splitTextToSize(line, CW);
      doc.text(wrapped, M, y);
      y += wrapped.length * lineH + 2;
    }
  }

  /* ═══════ FOOTER ON EVERY PAGE ═══════ */
  const total = doc.getNumberOfPages();
  for (let p = 1; p <= total; p++) {
    doc.setPage(p);

    // Skip footer on cover page (page 1) — keep it clean
    if (p === 1) continue;

    doc.setDrawColor(200, 200, 200);
    doc.setLineWidth(0.2);
    doc.line(M, PH - 14, PW - M, PH - 14);

    doc.setTextColor(...MUTED);
    doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
    doc.setFontSize(8);
    doc.text('Generated by Red Whale V1', M, PH - 8);
    doc.text(`Page ${p - 1} of ${total - 1}`, PW - M - 28, PH - 8);
  }

  return doc.output('datauristring');
}

export function downloadPDF(dataUri: string, filename = 'red-whale-document.pdf'): void {
  const link = document.createElement('a');
  link.href = dataUri;
  link.download = filename;
  link.click();
}
```

```
// PDF Generator — Premium beautiful PDFs with Red Whale branding
import { jsPDF } from 'jspdf';

/* ─── helpers ─── */

// Strip all formatting, markdown, and weird unicode artifacts
function cleanText(text: string): string {
  return (
    text
      // code blocks
      .replace(/```[\s\S]*?```/g, '')
      // inline code
      .replace(/`([^`]*)`/g, '$1')
      // bold / italic / underline markdown
      .replace(/\*\*([^*]+)\*\*/g, '$1')
      .replace(/\*([^*]+)\*/g, '$1')
      .replace(/__([^_]+)__/g, '$1')
      .replace(/_([^_]+)_/g, '$1')
      // heading hashes
      .replace(/^#{1,6}\s+/gm, '')
      // bullet / list markers
      .replace(/^\s*[•\-\*]\s+/gm, '')
      .replace(/^\s*\d+\.\s+/gm, '')
      // markdown links → just text
      .replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\([^)]+\)/g, '$1')
      .replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\[[^\]]*\]/g, '$1')
      // bare URLs
      .replace(/https?:\/\/[^\s]+/g, '')
      // table pipes & separator lines
      .replace(/\|/g, '')
      .replace(/^\s*[-:]+[-\s:]*\s*$/gm, '')
      // Remove ALL private-use / control / combining / unusual Unicode
      // Keep: Basic Latin, Latin-1, Devanagari, CJK, common symbols
      .replace(/[\uE000-\uF8FF]/g, '')   // Private Use Area
      .replace(/[\uFFF0-\uFFFF]/g, '')   // Specials
      .replace(/[\u0080-\u009F]/g, '')   // C1 controls
      .replace(/[\u0600-\u06FF]/g, '')   // Arabic
      .replace(/[\u0E00-\u0E7F]/g, '')   // Thai
      .replace(/[\u0370-\u03FF]/g, '')   // Greek
      .replace(/[\u0400-\u04FF]/g, '')   // Cyrillic
      .replace(/[\u0100-\u017F]/g, '')   // Latin Extended-A
      .replace(/[\u0180-\u024F]/g, '')   // Latin Extended-B
      .replace(/[\u0300-\u036F]/g, '')   // Combining diacritical marks
      // Remove weird letter-by-letter spaced words (e.g. "M U S T :"  or "c a k e")
      .replace(/\b([A-Za-z])\s(?=\s*[A-Za-z]\b)/g, '')
      .replace(/\b([A-Za-z]) (?=[A-Za-z]\b)/g, '')
      // Clean extra whitespace
      .replace(/[ \t]+/g, ' ')
      .replace(/\n{3,}/g, '\n\n')
      .trim()
  );
}

function getDateStr(): string {
  const d = new Date();
  return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
    year: 'numeric',
    month: 'long',
    day: 'numeric',
  });
}

/* ─── detect whether a PDF button should show ─── */
export function isStructuredContent(text: string): boolean {
  const hasTable = /\|.+/m.test(text);
  const hasSchedule = /\b(monday|tuesday|wednesday|thursday|friday|saturday|sunday|time|schedule|timetable|routine|plan|report|summary|table|chart|list|ingredient|step|material)\b/i.test(text);
  const hasHeadings = /^#{1,6}\s+/m.test(text);
  const hasLists = /^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/m.test(text);
  return hasTable || (hasSchedule && (hasHeadings || hasLists));
}

/* ─── main PDF builder ─── */
export async function generatePDF(rawContent: string, title = 'Red Whale Document'): Promise<string> {
  const doc = new jsPDF({ orientation: 'portrait', unit: 'mm', format: 'a4' });

  const PW = doc.internal.pageSize.getWidth();   // 210
  const PH = doc.internal.pageSize.getHeight();  // 297
  const M = 20;                                    // margin
  const CW = PW - M * 2;                           // content width

  const content = cleanText(rawContent);
  const docTitle = cleanText(title).slice(0, 60);

  /* ═══════ PAGE 1 — COVER ═══════ */
  // Red top banner
  doc.setFillColor(185, 28, 28); // red-700
  doc.rect(0, 0, PW, 55, 'F');

  // Subtle bottom edge of banner
  doc.setFillColor(127, 29, 29); // red-900
  doc.rect(0, 53, PW, 2, 'F');

  // "RED WHALE" on cover
  doc.setTextColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(28);
  doc.text('RED WHALE', M, 28);

  // Subtitle
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'italic');
  doc.setFontSize(11);
  doc.text('AI-Powered Intelligence', M, 37);

  // Decorative circle on right side of banner
  doc.setDrawColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.8);
  doc.circle(PW - M - 12, 30, 8, 'S');
  doc.circle(PW - M - 12, 30, 4, 'S');

  // Document title (below banner)
  let y = 70;
  doc.setTextColor(31, 41, 55);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(20);
  const titleLines = doc.splitTextToSize(docTitle, CW);
  doc.text(titleLines, M, y);
  y += titleLines.length * 8 + 2;

  // Red accent line under title
  doc.setDrawColor(185, 28, 28);
  doc.setLineWidth(1);
  const tw = doc.getTextWidth(docTitle);
  doc.line(M, y, M + Math.min(tw, CW), y);
  y += 10;

  // Date
  doc.setTextColor(107, 114, 128);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
  doc.setFontSize(10);
  doc.text(getDateStr(), M, y);
  y += 14;

  // Horizontal divider
  doc.setDrawColor(200, 200, 200);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.2);
  doc.line(M, y, PW - M, y);
  y += 10;

  /* ═══════ CONTENT PAGES ═══════ */
  const bodyLines = content.split('\n');

  for (const raw of bodyLines) {
    const line = raw.trim();
    if (!line) {
      y += 4;
      continue;
    }

    // ── Detect section headings ──
    // Heuristic: short (<55 chars), ≤6 words, no lowercase starting words
    const words = line.split(/\s+/);
    const looksLikeHeading =
      line.length < 55 &&
      words.length <= 8 &&
      /^[A-Z0-9]/.test(line) &&
      !/\b(and|the|for|with|from|into|onto|upon|this|that|these|those|when|where|because|since|while|during|before|after|above|below|between|under|over|again|further|then|once|here|there|all|any|both|each|few|more|most|other|some|such|no|nor|not|only|own|same|so|than|too|very|can|will|just|should|now)\b/i.test(words[0] || '');

    // Page break
    const lineH = looksLikeHeading ? 5.5 : 4.8;
    const needed = looksLikeHeading ? 14 : 6;
    if (y + needed > PH - M - 10) {
      doc.addPage();
      y = M;
    }

    if (looksLikeHeading) {
      // Small red square bullet
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.rect(M, y - 2.5, 3, 3, 'F');

      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
      doc.setFontSize(12);
      doc.setTextColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.text(line, M + 5, y);
      y += 10;
    } else {
      // Body text
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
      doc.setFontSize(10);
      doc.setTextColor(DARK_R, DARK_G, DARK_B);

      const wrapped = doc.splitTextToSize(line, CW);
      doc.text(wrapped, M, y);
      y += wrapped.length * lineH + 2;
    }
  }

  /* ═══════ FOOTER ON EVERY PAGE ═══════ */
  const total = doc.getNumberOfPages();
  for (let p = 1; p <= total; p++) {
    doc.setPage(p);

    // Skip footer on cover page (page 1) — keep it clean
    if (p === 1) continue;

    doc.setDrawColor(200, 200, 200);
    doc.setLineWidth(0.2);
    doc.line(M, PH - 14, PW - M, PH - 14);

    doc.setTextColor(MUTED_R, MUTED_G, MUTED_B);
    doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
    doc.setFontSize(8);
    doc.text('Generated by Red Whale V1', M, PH - 8);
    doc.text(`Page ${p - 1} of ${total - 1}`, PW - M - 28, PH - 8);
  }

  return doc.output('datauristring');
}

export function downloadPDF(dataUri: string, filename = 'red-whale-document.pdf'): void {
  const link = document.createElement('a');
  link.href = dataUri;
  link.download = filename;
  link.click();
}
```

```
// PDF Generator — Premium beautiful PDFs with Red Whale branding
import { jsPDF } from 'jspdf';

/* ─── helpers ─── */

// Aggressive text cleaning — remove markdown, weird unicode, spaced-out letters
function cleanText(text: string): string {
  return (
    text
      // code blocks
      .replace(/```[\s\S]*?```/g, '')
      // inline code
      .replace(/`([^`]*)`/g, '$1')
      // bold / italic / underline markdown
      .replace(/\*\*([^*]+)\*\*/g, '$1')
      .replace(/\*([^*]+)\*/g, '$1')
      .replace(/__([^_]+)__/g, '$1')
      .replace(/_([^_]+)_/g, '$1')
      // heading hashes
      .replace(/^#{1,6}\s+/gm, '')
      // bullet / list markers
      .replace(/^\s*[•\-\*]\s+/gm, '')
      .replace(/^\s*\d+\.\s+/gm, '')
      // markdown links → just text
      .replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\([^)]+\)/g, '$1')
      .replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\[[^\]]*\]/g, '$1')
      // bare URLs
      .replace(/https?:\/\/[^\s]+/g, '')
      // table pipes & separator lines
      .replace(/\|/g, '')
      .replace(/^\s*[-:]+[-\s:]*\s*$/gm, '')
      // ═══ AGGRESSIVE: strip weird model-inserted Unicode markers ═══
      // Latin-1 symbols often used as fake emoji / markers
      .replace(/[\u0080-\u00BF]/g, '')   // C1 + top-half Latin-1 (Ø Ý Ü ß ¯ ¡ etc.)
      .replace(/[\u00C0-\u00DF]/g, '')   // Latin-1 upper accented + math (keep lower if needed? no, strip all)
      // Actually keep useful Latin-1 lower half for common chars; strip the rest selectively:
      .replace(/[ØøÝýÿÜüß¿¡¯¨´¸ˆ˜]/g, '')
      // Private Use Area + specials
      .replace(/[\uE000-\uF8FF]/g, '')
      .replace(/[\uFFF0-\uFFFF]/g, '')
      // C1 controls
      .replace(/[\u0080-\u009F]/g, '')
      // Combining marks
      .replace(/[\u0300-\u036F]/g, '')
      // ═══ Collapse spaced single letters "M U S T" → "MUST", "c a k e" → "cake" ═══
      // Replace sequences of "L e t t e r" spaced by single spaces
      .replace(/\b([A-Za-z]) (?=[A-Za-z]\b)/g, '')
      // Clean extra whitespace
      .replace(/[ \t]+/g, ' ')
      .replace(/\n{3,}/g, '\n\n')
      .trim()
  );
}

function getDateStr(): string {
  const d = new Date();
  return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' });
}

/* ─── detect whether a PDF button should show ─── */
export function isStructuredContent(text: string): boolean {
  const hasTable = /\|.+/m.test(text);
  const hasSchedule = /\b(monday|tuesday|wednesday|thursday|friday|saturday|sunday|time|schedule|timetable|routine|plan|report|summary|table|chart|list|ingredient|step|material|recipe|steps|ingredients)\b/i.test(text);
  const hasHeadings = /^#{1,6}\s+/m.test(text);
  const hasLists = /^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/m.test(text);
  return hasTable || (hasSchedule && (hasHeadings || hasLists));
}

/* ─── main PDF builder ─── */
export async function generatePDF(rawContent: string, title = 'Red Whale Document'): Promise<string> {
  const doc = new jsPDF({ orientation: 'portrait', unit: 'mm', format: 'a4' });

  const PW = doc.internal.pageSize.getWidth();
  const PH = doc.internal.pageSize.getHeight();
  const M = 20;
  const CW = PW - M * 2;

  const content = cleanText(rawContent);
  const docTitle = cleanText(title).slice(0, 60);

  const RED = { r: 185, g: 28, b: 28 };
  const DARK = { r: 31, g: 41, b: 55 };
  const MUTED = { r: 107, g: 114, b: 128 };
  const GRAY_50 = { r: 249, g: 250, b: 251 };

  /* ═══════ PAGE 1 — COVER ═══════ */
  // Red top banner
  doc.setFillColor(RED.r, RED.g, RED.b);
  doc.rect(0, 0, PW, 55, 'F');
  doc.setFillColor(127, 29, 29);
  doc.rect(0, 53, PW, 2, 'F');

  doc.setTextColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(28);
  doc.text('RED WHALE', M, 28);

  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'italic');
  doc.setFontSize(11);
  doc.text('AI-Powered Intelligence', M, 37);

  // Decorative circle on right side of banner
  doc.setDrawColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.8);
  doc.circle(PW - M - 12, 30, 8, 'S');
  doc.circle(PW - M - 12, 30, 4, 'S');

  // Document title (below banner)
  let y = 70;
  doc.setTextColor(DARK.r, DARK.g, DARK.b);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(20);
  const titleLines = doc.splitTextToSize(docTitle, CW);
  doc.text(titleLines, M, y);
  y += titleLines.length * 8 + 2;

  // Red accent line under title
  doc.setDrawColor(RED.r, RED.g, RED.b);
  doc.setLineWidth(1);
  const tw = doc.getTextWidth(docTitle);
  doc.line(M, y, M + Math.min(tw, CW), y);
  y += 10;

  // Date
  doc.setTextColor(MUTED.r, MUTED.g, MUTED.b);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
  doc.setFontSize(10);
  doc.text(getDateStr(), M, y);
  y += 14;

  // Horizontal divider
  doc.setDrawColor(200, 200, 200);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.2);
  doc.line(M, y, PW - M, y);
  y += 10;

  /* ═══════ CONTENT PAGES ═══════ */
  const bodyLines = content.split('\n');

  for (const raw of bodyLines) {
    const line = raw.trim();
    if (!line) {
      y += 4;
      continue;
    }

    // Heading heuristic: short, ≤8 words, starts capital, not a common sentence word
    const words = line.split(/\s+/);
    const looksLikeHeading =
      line.length < 55 &&
      words.length <= 8 &&
      /^[A-Z0-9]/.test(line) &&
      !/\b(and|the|for|with|from|into|onto|upon|this|that|these|those|when|where|because|since|while|during|before|after|above|below|between|under|over|again|further|then|once|here|there|all|any|both|each|few|more|most|other|some|such|no|nor|not|only|own|same|so|than|too|very|can|will|just|should|now)\b/i.test(words[0] || '');

    const lineH = looksLikeHeading ? 5.5 : 4.8;
    const needed = looksLikeHeading ? 16 : 6;
    if (y + needed > PH - M - 10) {
      doc.addPage();
      // Light gray page background on content pages for premium feel
      doc.setFillColor(GRAY_50.r, GRAY_50.g, GRAY_50.b);
      doc.rect(0, 0, PW, PH, 'F');
      y = M;
    }

    if (looksLikeHeading) {
      // Section card background
      doc.setFillColor(254, 242, 242); // red-50
      doc.roundedRect(M - 2, y - 6, CW + 4, 10, 1, 1, 'F');

      // Red vertical bar
      doc.setFillColor(RED.r, RED.g, RED.b);
      doc.rect(M - 2, y - 6, 2, 10, 'F');

      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
      doc.setFontSize(12);
      doc.setTextColor(RED.r, RED.g, RED.b);
      doc.text(line, M + 2, y);
      y += 12;
    } else {
      // Body text
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
      doc.setFontSize(10);
      doc.setTextColor(DARK.r, DARK.g, DARK.b);

      const wrapped = doc.splitTextToSize(line, CW);
      doc.text(wrapped, M, y);
      y += wrapped.length * lineH + 2;
    }
  }

  /* ═══════ FOOTER ON CONTENT PAGES ═══════ */
  const total = doc.getNumberOfPages();
  for (let p = 1; p <= total; p++) {
    doc.setPage(p);
    if (p === 1) continue; // cover stays clean

    doc.setDrawColor(200, 200, 200);
    doc.setLineWidth(0.2);
    doc.line(M, PH - 14, PW - M, PH - 14);

    doc.setTextColor(MUTED.r, MUTED.g, MUTED.b);
    doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
    doc.setFontSize(8);
    doc.text('Generated by Red Whale V1', M, PH - 8);
    doc.text(`Page ${p - 1} of ${total - 1}`, PW - M - 28, PH - 8);
  }

  return doc.output('datauristring');
}

export function downloadPDF(dataUri: string, filename = 'red-whale-document.pdf'): void {
  const link = document.createElement('a');
  link.href = dataUri;
  link.download = filename;
  link.click();
}
```

// PDF Generator — Premium beautiful PDFs with Red Whale branding
import { jsPDF } from 'jspdf';

/* ─── helpers ─── */

// Strip all formatting, markdown, and weird unicode artifacts
function cleanText(text: string): string {
  return (
    text
      // code blocks
      .replace(/```[\s\S]*?```/g, '')
      // inline code
      .replace(/`([^`]*)`/g, '$1')
      // bold / italic / underline markdown
      .replace(/\*\*([^*]+)\*\*/g, '$1')
      .replace(/\*([^*]+)\*/g, '$1')
      .replace(/__([^_]+)__/g, '$1')
      .replace(/_([^_]+)_/g, '$1')
      // heading hashes
      .replace(/^#{1,6}\s+/gm, '')
      // bullet / list markers
      .replace(/^\s*[•\-\*]\s+/gm, '')
      .replace(/^\s*\d+\.\s+/gm, '')
      // markdown links → just text
      .replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\([^)]+\)/g, '$1')
      .replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\[[^\]]*\]/g, '$1')
      // bare URLs
      .replace(/https?:\/\/[^\s]+/g, '')
      // table pipes & separator lines
      .replace(/\|/g, '')
      .replace(/^\s*[-:]+[-\s:]*\s*$/gm, '')
      // Remove ALL private-use / control / combining / unusual Unicode
      // Keep: Basic Latin, Latin-1, Devanagari, CJK, common symbols
      .replace(/[\uE000-\uF8FF]/g, '')   // Private Use Area
      .replace(/[\uFFF0-\uFFFF]/g, '')   // Specials
      .replace(/[\u0080-\u009F]/g, '')   // C1 controls
      .replace(/[\u0600-\u06FF]/g, '')   // Arabic
      .replace(/[\u0E00-\u0E7F]/g, '')   // Thai
      .replace(/[\u0370-\u03FF]/g, '')   // Greek
      .replace(/[\u0400-\u04FF]/g, '')   // Cyrillic
      .replace(/[\u0100-\u017F]/g, '')   // Latin Extended-A
      .replace(/[\u0180-\u024F]/g, '')   // Latin Extended-B
      .replace(/[\u0300-\u036F]/g, '')   // Combining diacritical marks
      // Remove weird letter-by-letter spaced words (e.g. "M U S T :"  or "c a k e")
      .replace(/\b([A-Za-z])\s(?=\s*[A-Za-z]\b)/g, '')
      .replace(/\b([A-Za-z]) (?=[A-Za-z]\b)/g, '')
      // Clean extra whitespace
      .replace(/[ \t]+/g, ' ')
      .replace(/\n{3,}/g, '\n\n')
      .trim()
  );
}

function getDateStr(): string {
  const d = new Date();
  return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
    year: 'numeric',
    month: 'long',
    day: 'numeric',
  });
}

/* ─── detect whether a PDF button should show ─── */
export function isStructuredContent(text: string): boolean {
  const hasTable = /\|.+/m.test(text);
  const hasSchedule = /\b(monday|tuesday|wednesday|thursday|friday|saturday|sunday|time|schedule|timetable|routine|plan|report|summary|table|chart|list|ingredient|step|material)\b/i.test(text);
  const hasHeadings = /^#{1,6}\s+/m.test(text);
  const hasLists = /^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/m.test(text);
  return hasTable || (hasSchedule && (hasHeadings || hasLists));
}

/* ─── main PDF builder ─── */
export async function generatePDF(rawContent: string, title = 'Red Whale Document'): Promise<string> {
  const doc = new jsPDF({ orientation: 'portrait', unit: 'mm', format: 'a4' });

  const PW = doc.internal.pageSize.getWidth();   // 210
  const PH = doc.internal.pageSize.getHeight();  // 297
  const M = 20;                                    // margin
  const CW = PW - M * 2;                           // content width

  const content = cleanText(rawContent);
  const docTitle = cleanText(title).slice(0, 60);

  /* ═══════ PAGE 1 — COVER ═══════ */
  // Red top banner
  doc.setFillColor(185, 28, 28); // red-700
  doc.rect(0, 0, PW, 55, 'F');

  // Subtle bottom edge of banner
  doc.setFillColor(127, 29, 29); // red-900
  doc.rect(0, 53, PW, 2, 'F');

  // "RED WHALE" on cover
  doc.setTextColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(28);
  doc.text('RED WHALE', M, 28);

  // Subtitle
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'italic');
  doc.setFontSize(11);
  doc.text('AI-Powered Intelligence', M, 37);

  // Decorative circle on right side of banner
  doc.setDrawColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.8);
  doc.circle(PW - M - 12, 30, 8, 'S');
  doc.circle(PW - M - 12, 30, 4, 'S');

  const RED_R = 185, RED_G = 28, RED_B = 28;
  const DARK_R = 31, DARK_G = 41, DARK_B = 55;
  const MUTED_R = 107, MUTED_G = 114, MUTED_B = 128;

  // Document title (below banner)
  let y = 70;
  doc.setTextColor(31, 41, 55);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(20);
  const titleLines = doc.splitTextToSize(docTitle, CW);
  doc.text(titleLines, M, y);
  y += titleLines.length * 8 + 2;

  // Red accent line under title
  doc.setDrawColor(185, 28, 28);
  doc.setLineWidth(1);
  const tw = doc.getTextWidth(docTitle);
  doc.line(M, y, M + Math.min(tw, CW), y);
  y += 10;

  // Date
  doc.setTextColor(107, 114, 128);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
  doc.setFontSize(10);
  doc.text(getDateStr(), M, y);
  y += 14;

  // Horizontal divider
  doc.setDrawColor(200, 200, 200);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.2);
  doc.line(M, y, PW - M, y);
  y += 10;

  /* ═══════ CONTENT PAGES ═══════ */
  const bodyLines = content.split('\n');

  for (const raw of bodyLines) {
    const line = raw.trim();
    if (!line) {
      y += 4;
      continue;
    }

    // ── Detect section headings ──
    // Heuristic: short (<55 chars), ≤6 words, no lowercase starting words
    const words = line.split(/\s+/);
    const looksLikeHeading =
      line.length < 55 &&
      words.length <= 8 &&
      /^[A-Z0-9]/.test(line) &&
      !/\b(and|the|for|with|from|into|onto|upon|this|that|these|those|when|where|because|since|while|during|before|after|above|below|between|under|over|again|further|then|once|here|there|all|any|both|each|few|more|most|other|some|such|no|nor|not|only|own|same|so|than|too|very|can|will|just|should|now)\b/i.test(words[0] || '');

    // Page break
    const lineH = looksLikeHeading ? 5.5 : 4.8;
    const needed = looksLikeHeading ? 14 : 6;
    if (y + needed > PH - M - 10) {
      doc.addPage();
      y = M;
    }

    if (looksLikeHeading) {
      // Small red square bullet
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.rect(M, y - 2.5, 3, 3, 'F');

      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
      doc.setFontSize(12);
      doc.setTextColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.text(line, M + 5, y);
      y += 10;
    } else {
      // Body text
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
      doc.setFontSize(10);
      doc.setTextColor(DARK_R, DARK_G, DARK_B);

      const wrapped = doc.splitTextToSize(line, CW);
      doc.text(wrapped, M, y);
      y += wrapped.length * lineH + 2;
    }
  }

  /* ═══════ FOOTER ON EVERY PAGE ═══════ */
  const total = doc.getNumberOfPages();
  for (let p = 1; p <= total; p++) {
    doc.setPage(p);

    // Skip footer on cover page (page 1) — keep it clean
    if (p === 1) continue;

    doc.setDrawColor(200, 200, 200);
    doc.setLineWidth(0.2);
    doc.line(M, PH - 14, PW - M, PH - 14);

    doc.setTextColor(MUTED_R, MUTED_G, MUTED_B);
    doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
    doc.setFontSize(8);
    doc.text('Generated by Red Whale V1', M, PH - 8);
    doc.text(`Page ${p - 1} of ${total - 1}`, PW - M - 28, PH - 8);
  }

  return doc.output('datauristring');
}

  const link = document.createElement('a');
  link.href = dataUri;
  link.download = filename;
  link.click();

```
    doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
    doc.setFontSize(8);
    doc.text('Generated by Red Whale V1', M, PH - 8);
    doc.text(`Page ${p - 1} of ${total - 1}`, PW - M - 28, PH - 8);
  }

  return doc.output('datauristring');
}

export function downloadPDF(dataUri: string, filename = 'red-whale-document.pdf'): void {
  const link = document.createElement('a');
  link.href = dataUri;
  link.download = filename;
  link.click();
}
```
