// PDF Generator — Premium beautiful PDFs with Red Whale branding
import { jsPDF } from 'jspdf';

/* ─── helpers ─── */

function cleanText(text: string): string {
  let t = text;
  // 1. Remove code blocks & inline code
  t = t.replace(/```[\s\S]*?```/g, '');
  t = t.replace(/`([^`]*)`/g, '$1');
  // 2. Remove markdown formatting
  t = t.replace(/\*\*([^*]+)\*\*/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/\*([^*]+)\*/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/__([^_]+)__/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/_([^_]+)_/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/^#{1,6}\s+/gm, '');
  // 3. Remove list markers (keep the text)
  t = t.replace(/^\s*[•\-\*]\s+/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*\d+\.\s+/gm, '');
  // 4. Links → text only
  t = t.replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\([^)]+\)/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\[[^\]]*\]/g, '$1');
  // 5. URLs
  t = t.replace(/https?:\/\/[^\s]+/g, '');
  // 6. Table artifacts
  t = t.replace(/\|/g, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*[-:]+[-\s:]*\s*$/gm, '');
  // 7. AGGRESSIVE: strip any non-safe characters
  // Safe = ASCII printable (U+0020–U+007E) + Devanagari (U+0900–U+097F) + selected Latin-1
  t = t.replace(/[^\u0020-\u007E\u0900-\u097F\u00A0\u00A1\u00B0\u00B1\u00B4\u00B5\u00B6\u00B7\u00B8\u00B9\u00BA\u00BB\u00BC\u00BD\u00BE\u00BF\u00C0-\u00D6\u00D8-\u00F6\u00F8-\u00FF\n\r\t]/g, '');
  // 8. Strip common model marker patterns: =N, <word, >word at line starts
  t = t.replace(/^\s*=?\d+\s*/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*[<>=]+\s*/gm, '');
  // 9. Collapse spaced single letters: "M U S T" → "MUST"
  let prev;
  do {
    prev = t;
    t = t.replace(/\b([A-Za-z])\s+([A-Za-z]\b)/g, '$1$2');
  } while (t !== prev);
  // 10. Clean whitespace
  t = t.replace(/[ \t]+/g, ' ');
  t = t.replace(/\n{3,}/g, '\n\n');
  return t.trim();
}

function getDateStr(): string {
  const d = new Date();
  return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' });
}

/* ─── detect whether a PDF button should show ─── */
export function isStructuredContent(text: string): boolean {
  const hasTable = /\|.+/m.test(text);
  const hasSchedule = /\b(monday|tuesday|wednesday|thursday|friday|saturday|sunday|time|schedule|timetable|routine|plan|report|summary|table|chart|list|ingredient|step|material|recipe|steps|ingredients)\b/i.test(text);
  const hasHeadings = /^#{1,6}\s+/m.test(text);
  const hasLists = /^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/m.test(text);
  return hasTable || (hasSchedule && (hasHeadings || hasLists));
}

/* ─── main PDF builder ─── */
export async function generatePDF(rawContent: string, title = 'Red Whale Document'): Promise<string> {
  const doc = new jsPDF({ orientation: 'portrait', unit: 'mm', format: 'a4' });

  const PW = doc.internal.pageSize.getWidth();   // 210
  const PH = doc.internal.pageSize.getHeight();  // 297
  const M = 20;
  const CW = PW - M * 2;

  const content = cleanText(rawContent);
  const docTitle = cleanText(title).slice(0, 60);

  const RED_R = 185, RED_G = 28, RED_B = 28;
  const DARK_R = 31, DARK_G = 41, DARK_B = 55;
  const MUTED_R = 107, MUTED_G = 114, MUTED_B = 128;

  /* ═══════ COVER PAGE ═══════ */
  // Full red top banner
  doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
  doc.rect(0, 0, PW, 58, 'F');
  doc.setFillColor(127, 29, 29);
  doc.rect(0, 56, PW, 2, 'F');

  // Brand text
  doc.setTextColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(30);
  doc.text('RED WHALE', M, 30);

  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'italic');
  doc.setFontSize(12);
  doc.text('AI-Powered Intelligence', M, 40);

  // Decorative rings on right
  doc.setDrawColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setLineWidth(1);
  doc.circle(PW - M - 14, 32, 10, 'S');
  doc.circle(PW - M - 14, 32, 5, 'S');

  // Title block
  let y = 74;
  doc.setTextColor(DARK_R, DARK_G, DARK_B);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(22);
  const titleLines = doc.splitTextToSize(docTitle, CW);
  doc.text(titleLines, M, y);
  y += titleLines.length * 9 + 3;

  // Red accent underline
  doc.setDrawColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
  doc.setLineWidth(1.2);
  const tw = doc.getTextWidth(docTitle);
  doc.line(M, y, M + Math.min(tw, CW), y);
  y += 10;

  // Date
  doc.setTextColor(MUTED_R, MUTED_G, MUTED_B);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
  doc.setFontSize(11);
  doc.text(getDateStr(), M, y);
  y += 16;

  // Divider
  doc.setDrawColor(220, 220, 220);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.3);
  doc.line(M, y, PW - M, y);
  y += 12;

  /* ═══════ CONTENT PAGES ═══════ */
  const lines = content.split('\n');

  for (const raw of lines) {
    const line = raw.trim();
    if (!line) {
      y += 4;
      continue;
    }

    const words = line.split(/\s+/);
    const looksLikeHeading =
      line.length < 60 &&
      words.length <= 9 &&
      /^[A-Z0-9]/.test(line) &&
      !/\b(and|the|for|with|from|into|onto|upon|this|that|these|those|when|where|because|since|while|during|before|after|above|below|between|under|over|again|further|then|once|here|there|all|any|both|each|few|more|most|other|some|such|no|nor|not|only|own|same|so|than|too|very|can|will|just|should|now)\b/i.test(words[0] || '');

    const lineH = looksLikeHeading ? 5.5 : 4.8;
    const needed = looksLikeHeading ? 20 : 6;

    if (y + needed > PH - M - 10) {
      doc.addPage();
      // Light warm gray page fill
      doc.setFillColor(250, 250, 250);
      doc.rect(0, 0, PW, PH, 'F');
      y = M;
    }

    if (looksLikeHeading) {
      // Section card background
      doc.setFillColor(254, 242, 242);
      doc.roundedRect(M - 3, y - 7, CW + 6, 11, 1.5, 1.5, 'F');
      // Left red accent bar
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.rect(M - 3, y - 7, 2.5, 11, 'F');

      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
      doc.setFontSize(12);
      doc.setTextColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.text(line, M + 2, y);
      y += 14;
    } else {
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
      doc.setFontSize(10);
      doc.setTextColor(DARK_R, DARK_G, DARK_B);

      const wrapped = doc.splitTextToSize(line, CW);
      doc.text(wrapped, M, y);
      y += wrapped.length * lineH + 2;
    }
  }

  /* ═══════ FOOTER (skip cover) ═══════ */
  const total = doc.getNumberOfPages();
  for (let p = 1; p <= total; p++) {
    doc.setPage(p);
    if (p === 1) continue;

    doc.setDrawColor(210, 210, 210);
    doc.setLineWidth(0.2);
    doc.line(M, PH - 14, PW - M, PH - 14);

    doc.setTextColor(MUTED_R, MUTED_G, MUTED_B);
    doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
    doc.setFontSize(8);
    doc.text('Generated by Red Whale V1', M, PH - 8);
    doc.text(`Page ${p - 1} of ${total - 1}`, PW - M - 30, PH - 8);
  }

  return doc.output('datauristring');
}

export function downloadPDF(dataUri: string, filename = 'red-whale-document.pdf'): void {
  const link = document.createElement('a');
  link.href = dataUri;
  link.download = filename;
  link.click();
}

// PDF Generator — Premium beautiful PDFs with Red Whale branding
import { jsPDF } from 'jspdf';

/* ─── helpers ─── */

function cleanText(text: string): string {
  let t = text;
  // 1. Remove code blocks & inline code
  t = t.replace(/```[\s\S]*?```/g, '');
  t = t.replace(/`([^`]*)`/g, '$1');
  // 2. Remove markdown formatting
  t = t.replace(/\*\*([^*]+)\*\*/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/\*([^*]+)\*/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/__([^_]+)__/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/_([^_]+)_/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/^#{1,6}\s+/gm, '');
  // 3. Remove list markers (keep text)
  t = t.replace(/^\s*[•\-\*]\s+/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*\d+\.\s+/gm, '');
  // 4. Links → text only
  t = t.replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\([^)]+\)/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\[[^\]]*\]/g, '$1');
  // 5. URLs
  t = t.replace(/https?:\/\/[^\s]+/g, '');
  // 6. Table artifacts
  t = t.replace(/\|/g, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*[-:]+[-\s:]*\s*$/gm, '');
  // 7. Strip model marker characters (Ø, Ý, Ü, ß, ¯, ¡, ¿, ¨, ´, ¸, ˆ, ˜, ·, †, ‡, §, ¶, ‹, ›, «, », „, ", ', ‘, ’)
  t = t.replace(/[ØøÝýÿÜüß¿¡¯¨´¸ˆ˜·†‡§¶‹›«»„"“”‘’]/g, '');
  // 8. Strip remaining weird high-unicode blocks
  t = t.replace(/[\uE000-\uF8FF\uFFF0-\uFFFF\u0080-\u009F\u0300-\u036F]/g, '');
  // 9. Strip line-start markers like =4, <, >, =Ý, etc.
  t = t.replace(/^\s*=?\d*\s*/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*[<>=]+\s*/gm, '');
  // 10. Strip stray control chars
  t = t.replace(/[\x00-\x08\x0B\x0C\x0E-\x1F]/g, '');
  // 11. COLLAPSE spaced single letters: "B a k e" → "Bake", "M U S T" → "MUST"
  // If >50% of tokens in a line are single letters, collapse all spaces in that line
  const lines = t.split('\n');
  t = lines.map((line) => {
    const trimmed = line.trim();
    const tokens = trimmed.split(/\s+/);
    if (tokens.length >= 3) {
      const singleLetters = tokens.filter((tok) => /^[A-Za-z]$/.test(tok)).length;
      if (singleLetters / tokens.length > 0.4) {
        // Collapse all spaces in this line
        return trimmed.replace(/\s+/g, '');
      }
    }
    return line;
  }).join('\n');
  // 12. Clean whitespace
  t = t.replace(/[ \t]+/g, ' ');
  t = t.replace(/\n{3,}/g, '\n\n');
  return t.trim();
}

function getDateStr(): string {
  const d = new Date();
  return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' });
}

  const hasHeadings = /^#{1,6}\s+/m.test(text);
  const hasLists = /^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/m.test(text);
  return hasTable || (hasSchedule && (hasHeadings || hasLists));
}

// PDF Generator — Premium beautiful PDFs with Red Whale branding
import { jsPDF } from 'jspdf';

/* ─── helpers ─── */

// Whitelist of safe characters for PDF output
const SAFE_REGEX = /[^\u0020-\u007E\u0900-\u097F\u00B0\u00BD\u00A0\n\r\t]/g;

function cleanText(text: string): string {
  let t = text;
  // 1. Remove code blocks & inline code
  t = t.replace(/```[\s\S]*?```/g, '');
  t = t.replace(/`([^`]*)`/g, '$1');
  // 2. Remove markdown formatting
  t = t.replace(/\*\*([^*]+)\*\*/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/\*([^*]+)\*/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/__([^_]+)__/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/_([^_]+)_/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/^#{1,6}\s+/gm, '');
  // 3. Remove list markers (keep text)
  t = t.replace(/^\s*[•\-\*]\s+/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*\d+\.\s+/gm, '');
  // 4. Links → text only
  t = t.replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\([^)]+\)/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\[[^\]]*\]/g, '$1');
  // 5. URLs
  t = t.replace(/https?:\/\/[^\s]+/g, '');
  // 6. Table artifacts
  t = t.replace(/\|/g, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*[-:]+[-\s:]*\s*$/gm, '');
  // 7. AGGRESSIVE: strip every character not in safe whitelist
  t = t.replace(SAFE_REGEX, '');
  // 8. Strip line-start ASCII markers =N, <, >, =
  t = t.replace(/^\s*=?\d+\s*/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*[<>=]+\s*/gm, '');
  // 9. COLLAPSE spaced single letters: if >40% of tokens are single letters, remove all spaces
  const lines = t.split('\n');
  t = lines.map((line) => {
    const trimmed = line.trim();
    const tokens = trimmed.split(/\s+/);
    if (tokens.length >= 3) {
      const singleLetters = tokens.filter((tok) => /^[A-Za-z]$/.test(tok)).length;
      if (singleLetters / tokens.length > 0.4) {
        return trimmed.replace(/\s+/g, '');
      }
    }
    return line;
  }).join('\n');
  // 10. Clean whitespace
  t = t.replace(/[ \t]+/g, ' ');
  t = t.replace(/\n{3,}/g, '\n\n');
  return t.trim();
}

function getDateStr(): string {
  const d = new Date();
  return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' });
}

/* ─── detect whether a PDF button should show ─── */
export function isStructuredContent(text: string): boolean {
  const hasTable = /\|.+/m.test(text);
  const hasSchedule = /\b(monday|tuesday|wednesday|thursday|friday|saturday|sunday|time|schedule|timetable|routine|plan|report|summary|table|chart|list|ingredient|step|material|recipe|steps|ingredients)\b/i.test(text);
  const hasHeadings = /^#{1,6}\s+/m.test(text);
  const hasLists = /^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/m.test(text);
  return hasTable || (hasSchedule && (hasHeadings || hasLists));
}

/* ─── main PDF builder ─── */
export async function generatePDF(rawContent: string, title = 'Red Whale Document'): Promise<string> {
  const doc = new jsPDF({ orientation: 'portrait', unit: 'mm', format: 'a4' });

  const PW = doc.internal.pageSize.getWidth();
  const PH = doc.internal.pageSize.getHeight();
  const M = 20;
  const CW = PW - M * 2;

  const content = cleanText(rawContent);
  const docTitle = cleanText(title).slice(0, 60);

  const RED_R = 185, RED_G = 28, RED_B = 28;
  const DARK_R = 31, DARK_G = 41, DARK_B = 55;
  const MUTED_R = 107, MUTED_G = 114, MUTED_B = 128;

  /* ═══════ COVER PAGE ═══════ */
  // Full red top banner
  doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
  doc.rect(0, 0, PW, 58, 'F');
  doc.setFillColor(127, 29, 29);
  doc.rect(0, 56, PW, 2, 'F');

  // Brand text
  doc.setTextColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(30);
  doc.text('RED WHALE', M, 30);

  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'italic');
  doc.setFontSize(12);
  doc.text('AI-Powered Intelligence', M, 40);

  // Decorative rings on right
  doc.setDrawColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setLineWidth(1);
  doc.circle(PW - M - 14, 32, 10, 'S');
  doc.circle(PW - M - 14, 32, 5, 'S');

  // Title block
  let y = 74;
  doc.setTextColor(DARK_R, DARK_G, DARK_B);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(22);
  const titleLines = doc.splitTextToSize(docTitle, CW);
  doc.text(titleLines, M, y);
  y += titleLines.length * 9 + 3;

  // Red accent underline
  doc.setDrawColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
  doc.setLineWidth(1.2);
  const tw = doc.getTextWidth(docTitle);
  doc.line(M, y, M + Math.min(tw, CW), y);
  y += 10;

  // Date
  doc.setTextColor(MUTED_R, MUTED_G, MUTED_B);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
  doc.setFontSize(11);
  doc.text(getDateStr(), M, y);
  y += 16;

  // Divider
  doc.setDrawColor(220, 220, 220);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.3);
  doc.line(M, y, PW - M, y);
  y += 12;

  /* ═══════ CONTENT PAGES ═══════ */
  const lines = content.split('\n');

  for (const raw of lines) {
    const line = raw.trim();
    if (!line) {
      y += 4;
      continue;
    }

    const words = line.split(/\s+/);
    const looksLikeHeading =
      line.length < 60 &&
      words.length <= 9 &&
      /^[A-Z0-9]/.test(line) &&
      !/\b(and|the|for|with|from|into|onto|upon|this|that|these|those|when|where|because|since|while|during|before|after|above|below|between|under|over|again|further|then|once|here|there|all|any|both|each|few|more|most|other|some|such|no|nor|not|only|own|same|so|than|too|very|can|will|just|should|now)\b/i.test(words[0] || '');

    const lineH = looksLikeHeading ? 5.5 : 4.8;
    const needed = looksLikeHeading ? 20 : 6;

    if (y + needed > PH - M - 10) {
      doc.addPage();
      // Light warm gray page fill
      doc.setFillColor(250, 250, 250);
      doc.rect(0, 0, PW, PH, 'F');
      y = M;
    }

    if (looksLikeHeading) {
      // Section card background
      doc.setFillColor(254, 242, 242);
      doc.roundedRect(M - 3, y - 7, CW + 6, 11, 1.5, 1.5, 'F');
      // Left red accent bar
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.rect(M - 3, y - 7, 2.5, 11, 'F');

      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
      doc.setFontSize(12);
      doc.setTextColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.text(line, M + 2, y);
      y += 14;
    } else {
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
      doc.setFontSize(10);
      doc.setTextColor(DARK_R, DARK_G, DARK_B);

      const wrapped = doc.splitTextToSize(line, CW);
      doc.text(wrapped, M, y);
      y += wrapped.length * lineH + 2;
    }
  }

  /* ═══════ FOOTER (skip cover) ═══════ */
  const total = doc.getNumberOfPages();
  for (let p = 1; p <= total; p++) {
    doc.setPage(p);
    if (p === 1) continue;

    doc.setDrawColor(210, 210, 210);
    doc.setLineWidth(0.2);
    doc.line(M, PH - 14, PW - M, PH - 14);

    doc.setTextColor(MUTED_R, MUTED_G, MUTED_B);
    doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
    doc.setFontSize(8);
    doc.text('Generated by Red Whale V1', M, PH - 8);
    doc.text(`Page ${p - 1} of ${total - 1}`, PW - M - 30, PH - 8);
  }

  return doc.output('datauristring');
}

export function downloadPDF(dataUri: string, filename = 'red-whale-document.pdf'): void {
  const link = document.createElement('a');
  link.href = dataUri;
  link.download = filename;
  link.click();
}

// PDF Generator — Premium beautiful PDFs with Red Whale branding
import { jsPDF } from 'jspdf';

/* ─── helpers ─── */

const SAFE_REGEX = /[^\u0020-\u007E\u0900-\u097F\u00B0\u00BD\u00A0\n\r\t]/g;

function cleanText(text: string): string {
  let t = text;
  t = t.replace(/```[\s\S]*?```/g, '');
  t = t.replace(/`([^`]*)`/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/\*\*([^*]+)\*\*/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/\*([^*]+)\*/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/__([^_]+)__/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/_([^_]+)_/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/^#{1,6}\s+/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*[•\-\*]\s+/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*\d+\.\s+/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\([^)]+\)/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\[[^\]]*\]/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/https?:\/\/[^\s]+/g, '');
  t = t.replace(/\|/g, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*[-:]+[-\s:]*\s*$/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(SAFE_REGEX, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*=?\d+\s*/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*[<>=]+\s*/gm, '');
  const lines = t.split('\n');
  t = lines.map((line) => {
    const trimmed = line.trim();
    const tokens = trimmed.split(/\s+/);
    if (tokens.length >= 3) {
      const singleLetters = tokens.filter((tok) => /^[A-Za-z]$/.test(tok)).length;
      if (singleLetters / tokens.length > 0.4) {
        return trimmed.replace(/\s+/g, '');
      }
    }
    return line;
  }).join('\n');
  t = t.replace(/[ \t]+/g, ' ');
  t = t.replace(/\n{3,}/g, '\n\n');
  return t.trim();
}

function getDateStr(): string {
  const d = new Date();
  return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' });
}

function isBulletLine(line: string): boolean {
  return /^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/.test(line);
}

function isNumberedLine(line: string): boolean {
  return /^\s*\d+\.\s+/.test(line);
}

/* ─── detect whether a PDF button should show ─── */
export function isStructuredContent(text: string): boolean {
  const hasTable = /\|.+/m.test(text);
  const hasSchedule = /\b(monday|tuesday|wednesday|thursday|friday|saturday|sunday|time|schedule|timetable|routine|plan|report|summary|table|chart|list|ingredient|step|material|recipe|steps|ingredients)\b/i.test(text);
  const hasHeadings = /^#{1,6}\s+/m.test(text);
  const hasLists = /^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/m.test(text);
  return hasTable || (hasSchedule && (hasHeadings || hasLists));
}

/* ─── main PDF builder ─── */
export async function generatePDF(rawContent: string, title = 'Red Whale Document'): Promise<string> {
  const doc = new jsPDF({ orientation: 'portrait', unit: 'mm', format: 'a4' });

  const PW = doc.internal.pageSize.getWidth();
  const PH = doc.internal.pageSize.getHeight();
  const M = 20;
  const CW = PW - M * 2;

  const content = cleanText(rawContent);
  const docTitle = cleanText(title).slice(0, 60);

  const RED_R = 185, RED_G = 28, RED_B = 28;
  const DARK_R = 31, DARK_G = 41, DARK_B = 55;
  const MUTED_R = 107, MUTED_G = 114, MUTED_B = 128;

  /* ═══════ COVER PAGE ═══════ */
  // Red top banner
  doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
  doc.rect(0, 0, PW, 58, 'F');
  doc.setFillColor(127, 29, 29);
  doc.rect(0, 56, PW, 2, 'F');

  // Subtle decorative lines on banner
  doc.setDrawColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.3);
  for (let i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
    doc.line(PW - 50, 8 + i * 8, PW - 10, 8 + i * 8);
  }

  // Brand text
  doc.setTextColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(30);
  doc.text('RED WHALE', M, 30);

  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'italic');
  doc.setFontSize(12);
  doc.text('AI-Powered Intelligence', M, 40);

  // Decorative concentric circles on right
  doc.setDrawColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setLineWidth(1);
  doc.circle(PW - M - 14, 32, 10, 'S');
  doc.circle(PW - M - 14, 32, 5, 'S');
  doc.circle(PW - M - 14, 32, 2, 'F');

  // Title block
  let y = 74;
  doc.setTextColor(DARK_R, DARK_G, DARK_B);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(22);
  const titleLines = doc.splitTextToSize(docTitle, CW);
  doc.text(titleLines, M, y);
  y += titleLines.length * 9 + 3;

  // Red accent underline
  doc.setDrawColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
  doc.setLineWidth(1.2);
  const tw = doc.getTextWidth(docTitle);
  doc.line(M, y, M + Math.min(tw, CW), y);
  y += 10;

  // Date
  doc.setTextColor(MUTED_R, MUTED_G, MUTED_B);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
  doc.setFontSize(11);
  doc.text(getDateStr(), M, y);
  y += 16;

  // Divider
  doc.setDrawColor(220, 220, 220);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.3);
  doc.line(M, y, PW - M, y);
  y += 12;

  /* ═══════ CONTENT PAGES ═══════ */
  const lines = content.split('\n');

  for (const raw of lines) {
    const line = raw.trim();
    if (!line) {
      y += 4;
      continue;
    }

    const words = line.split(/\s+/);
    const looksLikeHeading =
      line.length < 60 &&
      words.length <= 9 &&
      /^[A-Z0-9]/.test(line) &&
      !/\b(and|the|for|with|from|into|onto|upon|this|that|these|those|when|where|because|since|while|during|before|after|above|below|between|under|over|again|further|then|once|here|there|all|any|both|each|few|more|most|other|some|such|no|nor|not|only|own|same|so|than|too|very|can|will|just|should|now)\b/i.test(words[0] || '');

    const isBullet = isBulletLine(raw);
    const isNumbered = isNumberedLine(raw);

    const lineH = looksLikeHeading ? 5.5 : 4.8;
    const needed = looksLikeHeading ? 20 : isBullet || isNumbered ? 10 : 6;

    if (y + needed > PH - M - 10) {
      doc.addPage();
      // Light warm gray page fill
      doc.setFillColor(250, 250, 250);
      doc.rect(0, 0, PW, PH, 'F');
      // Watermark
      doc.setTextColor(230, 230, 230);
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
      doc.setFontSize(40);
      const wm = 'RED WHALE';
      doc.text(wm, PW / 2, PH / 2, { align: 'center', angle: 45 });
      y = M;
    }

    if (looksLikeHeading) {
      // Section card background
      doc.setFillColor(254, 242, 242);
      doc.roundedRect(M - 3, y - 7, CW + 6, 11, 1.5, 1.5, 'F');
      // Left red accent bar
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.rect(M - 3, y - 7, 2.5, 11, 'F');

      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
      doc.setFontSize(12);
      doc.setTextColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.text(line, M + 2, y);
      y += 14;
    } else if (isBullet) {
      // Red square bullet
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.rect(M, y - 2, 2.5, 2.5, 'F');

      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
      doc.setFontSize(10);
      doc.setTextColor(DARK_R, DARK_G, DARK_B);

      const body = line.replace(/^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/, '');
      const wrapped = doc.splitTextToSize(body, CW - 6);
      doc.text(wrapped, M + 6, y);
      y += wrapped.length * lineH + 3;
    } else if (isNumbered) {
      const match = line.match(/^\s*(\d+)\.\s+(.*)/);
      const num = match ? match[1] : '';
      const body = match ? match[2] : line;

      // Red number circle
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.circle(M + 3, y - 1, 3, 'F');
      doc.setTextColor(255, 255, 255);
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
      doc.setFontSize(7);
      doc.text(num, M + 3, y, { align: 'center' });

      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
      doc.setFontSize(10);
      doc.setTextColor(DARK_R, DARK_G, DARK_B);

      const wrapped = doc.splitTextToSize(body, CW - 10);
      doc.text(wrapped, M + 10, y);
      y += wrapped.length * lineH + 3;
    } else {
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
      doc.setFontSize(10);
      doc.setTextColor(DARK_R, DARK_G, DARK_B);

      const wrapped = doc.splitTextToSize(line, CW);
      doc.text(wrapped, M, y);
      y += wrapped.length * lineH + 2;
    }
  }

  /* ═══════ FOOTER (skip cover) ═══════ */
  const total = doc.getNumberOfPages();
  for (let p = 1; p <= total; p++) {
    doc.setPage(p);
    if (p === 1) continue;

    // Footer line
    doc.setDrawColor(210, 210, 210);
    doc.setLineWidth(0.2);
    doc.line(M, PH - 14, PW - M, PH - 14);

    // Footer text
    doc.setTextColor(MUTED_R, MUTED_G, MUTED_B);
    doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
    doc.setFontSize(8);
    doc.text('Generated by Red Whale V1', M, PH - 8);

    // Page number circle
    doc.setDrawColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
    doc.setLineWidth(0.3);
    doc.circle(PW - M - 5, PH - 9, 4, 'S');
    doc.setTextColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
    doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
    doc.setFontSize(7);
    doc.text(`${p - 1}`, PW - M - 5, PH - 8, { align: 'center' });
  }

  return doc.output('datauristring');
}

export function downloadPDF(dataUri: string, filename = 'red-whale-document.pdf'): void {
  const link = document.createElement('a');
  link.href = dataUri;
  link.download = filename;
  link.click();
}

const SAFE = /[^\\u0020-\\u007E\\u0900-\\u097F\\u00B0\\u00BD\\u00A0\\n\\r\\t]/g;
function clean(t) {
  t = t.replace(/\`\`\`[\\s\\S]*?\`\`\`/g, '');
  t = t.replace(/\`([^\`]*)\`/g, '\$1');
  t = t.replace(/\\*\\*([^*]+)\\*\\*/g, '\$1');
  t = t.replace(/\\*([^*]+)\\*/g, '\$1');
  t = t.replace(/__([^_]+)__/g, '\$1');
  t = t.replace(/_([^_]+)_/g, '\$1');
  t = t.replace(/^#{1,6}\\s+/gm, '');
  // KEEP bullet markers for PDF detection
  t = t.replace(/^\\s*\\d+\\.\\s+/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(/\\[([^\\]]+)\\]\\([^)]+\\)/g, '\$1');
  t = t.replace(/\\[([^\\]]+)\\]\\[[^\\]]*\\]/g, '\$1');
  t = t.replace(/https?:\\/\\/[^\\s]+/g, '');
  t = t.replace(/\\|/g, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\\s*[-:]+[-\\s:]*\\s*$/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(SAFE, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\\s*=?\\d+\\s*/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\\s*[<>=]+\\s*/gm, '');
  const lines = t.split('\\n');
  t = lines.map((line) => {
    const trimmed = line.trim();
    const tokens = trimmed.split(/\\s+/);
    if (tokens.length >= 3) {
      const singleLetters = tokens.filter((tok) => /^[A-Za-z]\$/.test(tok)).length;
      if (singleLetters / tokens.length > 0.4) {
        return trimmed.replace(/\\s+/g, '');
      }
    }
    return line;
  }).join('\\n');
  t = t.replace(/[ \\t]+/g, ' ');
  t = t.replace(/\\n{3,}/g, '\\n\\n');
  return t.trim();
}

// PDF Generator — Premium beautiful PDFs with Red Whale branding
import { jsPDF } from 'jspdf';

/* ─── helpers ─── */

const SAFE_REGEX = /[^\u0020-\u007E\u0900-\u097F\u00B0\u00BD\u00A0\n\r\t]/g;

function cleanText(text: string): string {
  let t = text;
  t = t.replace(/```[\s\S]*?```/g, '');
  t = t.replace(/`([^`]*)`/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/\*\*([^*]+)\*\*/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/\*([^*]+)\*/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/__([^_]+)__/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/_([^_]+)_/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/^#{1,6}\s+/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\([^)]+\)/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\[[^\]]*\]/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/https?:\/\/[^\s]+/g, '');
  t = t.replace(/\|/g, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*[-:]+[-\s:]*\s*$/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(SAFE_REGEX, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*=?\d+\s*/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*[<>=]+\s*/gm, '');
  const lines = t.split('\n');
  t = lines.map((line) => {
    const trimmed = line.trim();
    const tokens = trimmed.split(/\s+/);
    if (tokens.length >= 3) {
      const singleLetters = tokens.filter((tok) => /^[A-Za-z]$/.test(tok)).length;
      if (singleLetters / tokens.length > 0.4) {
        return trimmed.replace(/\s+/g, '');
      }
    }
    return line;
  }).join('\n');
  t = t.replace(/[ \t]+/g, ' ');
  t = t.replace(/\n{3,}/g, '\n\n');
  return t.trim();
}

function getDateStr(): string {
  const d = new Date();
  return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' });
}

function isBulletLine(line: string): boolean {
  return /^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/.test(line);
}

function isNumberedLine(line: string): boolean {
  return /^\s*\d+\.\s+/.test(line);
}

/* ─── detect whether a PDF button should show ─── */
export function isStructuredContent(text: string): boolean {
  const hasTable = /\|.+/m.test(text);
  const hasSchedule = /\b(monday|tuesday|wednesday|thursday|friday|saturday|sunday|time|schedule|timetable|routine|plan|report|summary|table|chart|list|ingredient|step|material|recipe|steps|ingredients)\b/i.test(text);
  const hasHeadings = /^#{1,6}\s+/m.test(text);
  const hasLists = /^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/m.test(text);
  return hasTable || (hasSchedule && (hasHeadings || hasLists));
}

/* ─── main PDF builder ─── */
export async function generatePDF(rawContent: string, title = 'Red Whale Document'): Promise<string> {
  const doc = new jsPDF({ orientation: 'portrait', unit: 'mm', format: 'a4' });

  const PW = doc.internal.pageSize.getWidth();
  const PH = doc.internal.pageSize.getHeight();
  const M = 20;
  const CW = PW - M * 2;

  const content = cleanText(rawContent);
  const docTitle = cleanText(title).slice(0, 60);

  const RED_R = 185, RED_G = 28, RED_B = 28;
  const DARK_R = 31, DARK_G = 41, DARK_B = 55;
  const MUTED_R = 107, MUTED_G = 114, MUTED_B = 128;

  /* ═══════ COVER PAGE ═══════ */
  // Full red top banner
  doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
  doc.rect(0, 0, PW, 60, 'F');
  doc.setFillColor(127, 29, 29);
  doc.rect(0, 58, PW, 2, 'F');

  // Decorative horizontal lines on right side of banner
  doc.setDrawColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.3);
  for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
    doc.line(PW - 55, 6 + i * 8, PW - 8, 6 + i * 8);
  }

  // Brand text
  doc.setTextColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(32);
  doc.text('RED WHALE', M, 32);

  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'italic');
  doc.setFontSize(12);
  doc.text('AI-Powered Intelligence', M, 42);

  // Decorative concentric circles on right
  doc.setDrawColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setLineWidth(1);
  doc.circle(PW - M - 16, 34, 11, 'S');
  doc.circle(PW - M - 16, 34, 6, 'S');
  doc.setFillColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.circle(PW - M - 16, 34, 2.5, 'F');

  // Document title block
  let y = 78;
  doc.setTextColor(DARK_R, DARK_G, DARK_B);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(22);
  const titleLines = doc.splitTextToSize(docTitle, CW);
  doc.text(titleLines, M, y);
  y += titleLines.length * 9 + 3;

  // Red accent underline
  doc.setDrawColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
  doc.setLineWidth(1.2);
  const tw = doc.getTextWidth(docTitle);
  doc.line(M, y, M + Math.min(tw, CW), y);
  y += 10;

  // Date
  doc.setTextColor(MUTED_R, MUTED_G, MUTED_B);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
  doc.setFontSize(11);
  doc.text(getDateStr(), M, y);
  y += 18;

  // Divider
  doc.setDrawColor(220, 220, 220);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.3);
  doc.line(M, y, PW - M, y);
  y += 12;

  // "Premium Document" badge
  doc.setFillColor(254, 242, 242);
  doc.roundedRect(M, y, 55, 10, 2, 2, 'F');
  doc.setTextColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(9);
  doc.text('Premium Document', M + 4, y + 6.5);

  /* ═══════ CONTENT PAGES ═══════ */
  const lines = content.split('\n');

  for (const raw of lines) {
    const line = raw.trim();
    if (!line) {
      y += 4;
      continue;
    }

    const words = line.split(/\s+/);
    const looksLikeHeading =
      line.length < 60 &&
      words.length <= 9 &&
      /^[A-Z0-9]/.test(line) &&
      !/\b(and|the|for|with|from|into|onto|upon|this|that|these|those|when|where|because|since|while|during|before|after|above|below|between|under|over|again|further|then|once|here|there|all|any|both|each|few|more|most|other|some|such|no|nor|not|only|own|same|so|than|too|very|can|will|just|should|now)\b/i.test(words[0] || '');

    const isBullet = isBulletLine(raw);
    const isNumbered = isNumberedLine(raw);

    const lineH = looksLikeHeading ? 5.5 : 4.8;
    const needed = looksLikeHeading ? 20 : isBullet || isNumbered ? 10 : 6;

    if (y + needed > PH - M - 10) {
      doc.addPage();
      // Light warm gray page fill
      doc.setFillColor(250, 250, 250);
      doc.rect(0, 0, PW, PH, 'F');
      // Top red accent line
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.rect(0, 0, PW, 1.5, 'F');
      // Left margin red accent
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.rect(0, 0, 1.5, PH, 'F');
      // Watermark
      doc.setTextColor(240, 240, 240);
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
      doc.setFontSize(48);
      doc.text('RED WHALE', PW / 2, PH / 2, { align: 'center', angle: 45 });
      y = M;
    }

    if (looksLikeHeading) {
      // Section card background
      doc.setFillColor(254, 242, 242);
      doc.roundedRect(M - 3, y - 7, CW + 6, 11, 1.5, 1.5, 'F');
      // Left red accent bar
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.rect(M - 3, y - 7, 2.5, 11, 'F');

      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
      doc.setFontSize(12);
      doc.setTextColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.text(line, M + 2, y);
      y += 14;
    } else if (isBullet) {
      // Red square bullet
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.rect(M, y - 2, 2.5, 2.5, 'F');

      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
      doc.setFontSize(10);
      doc.setTextColor(DARK_R, DARK_G, DARK_B);

      const body = line.replace(/^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/, '');
      const wrapped = doc.splitTextToSize(body, CW - 6);
      doc.text(wrapped, M + 6, y);
      y += wrapped.length * lineH + 3;
    } else if (isNumbered) {
      const match = line.match(/^\s*(\d+)\.\s+(.*)/);
      const num = match ? match[1] : '';
      const body = match ? match[2] : line;

      // Red number circle
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.circle(M + 3, y - 1, 3, 'F');
      doc.setTextColor(255, 255, 255);
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
      doc.setFontSize(7);
      doc.text(num, M + 3, y, { align: 'center' });

      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
      doc.setFontSize(10);
      doc.setTextColor(DARK_R, DARK_G, DARK_B);

      const wrapped = doc.splitTextToSize(body, CW - 10);
      doc.text(wrapped, M + 10, y);
      y += wrapped.length * lineH + 3;
    } else {
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
      doc.setFontSize(10);
      doc.setTextColor(DARK_R, DARK_G, DARK_B);

      const wrapped = doc.splitTextToSize(line, CW);
      doc.text(wrapped, M, y);
      y += wrapped.length * lineH + 2;
    }
  }

  /* ═══════ FOOTER (skip cover) ═══════ */
  const total = doc.getNumberOfPages();
  for (let p = 1; p <= total; p++) {
    doc.setPage(p);
    if (p === 1) continue;

    // Footer line
    doc.setDrawColor(210, 210, 210);
    doc.setLineWidth(0.2);
    doc.line(M, PH - 14, PW - M, PH - 14);

    // Footer text
    doc.setTextColor(MUTED_R, MUTED_G, MUTED_B);
    doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
    doc.setFontSize(8);
    doc.text('Generated by Red Whale V1', M, PH - 8);

    // Page number circle
    doc.setDrawColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
    doc.setLineWidth(0.3);
    doc.circle(PW - M - 5, PH - 9, 4, 'S');
    doc.setTextColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
    doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
    doc.setFontSize(7);
    doc.text(`${p - 1}`, PW - M - 5, PH - 8, { align: 'center' });
  }

  return doc.output('datauristring');
}

export function downloadPDF(dataUri: string, filename = 'red-whale-document.pdf'): void {
  const link = document.createElement('a');
  link.href = dataUri;
  link.download = filename;
  link.click();
}

--BEGIN AGENT OBSERVATION--
// DownloadPDFButton — Premium PDF download for structured AI responses
import { useState, useCallback } from 'react';
import { FileDown, Loader2 } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { toast } from 'sonner';
import { generatePDF, downloadPDF, isStructuredContent } from '@/utils/pdfGenerator';

interface DownloadPDFButtonProps {
  content: string;
  title?: string;
}

export function DownloadPDFButton({ content, title = 'Red Whale Document' }: DownloadPDFButtonProps) {
  const [generating, setGenerating] = useState(false);

  const handleDownload = useCallback(async () => {
    if (generating) return;
    setGenerating(true);
    try {
      const dataUri = await generatePDF(content, title);
      const safeTitle = title.replace(/[^a-z0-9\u0900-\u097F\u4e00-\u9fff\uac00-\ud7af]/gi, '-').slice(0, 40);
      downloadPDF(dataUri, `${safeTitle || 'red-whale'}.pdf`);
      toast.success('PDF downloaded!');
    } catch {
      toast.error('Failed to generate PDF. Please try again.');
    }
    setGenerating(false);
  }, [content, title, generating]);

  if (!isStructuredContent(content)) return null;

  return (
    <Button
      variant="ghost"
      size="sm"
      onClick={handleDownload}
      disabled={generating}
      className="h-6 px-2 text-[10px] rounded-full text-primary hover:bg-primary/10"
      title="Download as PDF"
    >
      {generating ? (
        <><Loader2 className="w-3 h-3 mr-1 animate-spin" /> PDF…</>
      ) : (
        <><FileDown className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" /> PDF</>
      )}
    </Button>
  );
}

```
// PDF Generator — Premium beautiful PDFs with Red Whale branding
import { jsPDF } from 'jspdf';

/* ─── helpers ─── */

const SAFE_REGEX = /[^\u0020-\u007E\u0900-\u097F\u00B0\u00BD\u00A0\n\r\t]/g;

/** Smart single-letter word reconstruction.
 *  "M U S T : 1 ½ c u p s" → "MUST : 1 ½ cups"
 *  "B a k e a m o i s t"     → "Bakeamoist"  (best effort, model destroyed word boundaries)
 */
function collapseSpacedLetters(line: string): string {
  const trimmed = line.trim();
  const tokens = trimmed.split(/\s+/);
  if (tokens.length < 3) return line;

  const singleLetters = tokens.filter((t) => /^[A-Za-z]$/.test(t)).length;
  if (singleLetters / tokens.length <= 0.4) return line;

  // Merge consecutive runs of single letters, keep other tokens separate
  const out: string[] = [];
  let run: string[] = [];
  const flush = () => {
    if (run.length) { out.push(run.join('')); run = []; }
  };
  for (const tok of tokens) {
    if (/^[A-Za-z]$/.test(tok)) {
      run.push(tok);
    } else {
      flush();
      out.push(tok);
    }
  }
  flush();
  return out.join(' ');
}

function cleanText(text: string): string {
  let t = text;
  t = t.replace(/```[\s\S]*?```/g, '');
  t = t.replace(/`([^`]*)`/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/\*\*([^*]+)\*\*/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/\*([^*]+)\*/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/__([^_]+)__/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/_([^_]+)_/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/^#{1,6}\s+/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\([^)]+\)/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\[[^\]]*\]/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/https?:\/\/[^\s]+/g, '');
  t = t.replace(/\|/g, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*[-:]+[-\s:]*\s*$/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(SAFE_REGEX, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*=?\d+\s*/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*[<>=]+\s*/gm, '');
  // Collapse spaced single-letter words per line
  t = t.split('\n').map(collapseSpacedLetters).join('\n');
  t = t.replace(/[ \t]+/g, ' ');
  t = t.replace(/\n{3,}/g, '\n\n');
  return t.trim();
}

function getDateStr(): string {
  const d = new Date();
  return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' });
}

function isBulletLine(line: string): boolean {
  return /^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/.test(line);
}

function isNumberedLine(line: string): boolean {
  return /^\s*\d+\.\s+/.test(line);
}

/* ─── detect whether a PDF button should show ─── */
export function isStructuredContent(text: string): boolean {
  const hasTable = /\|.+/m.test(text);
  const hasSchedule = /\b(monday|tuesday|wednesday|thursday|friday|saturday|sunday|time|schedule|timetable|routine|plan|report|summary|table|chart|list|ingredient|step|material|recipe|steps|ingredients)\b/i.test(text);
  const hasHeadings = /^#{1,6}\s+/m.test(text);
  const hasLists = /^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/m.test(text);
  return hasTable || (hasSchedule && (hasHeadings || hasLists));
}

/* ─── main PDF builder ─── */
export async function generatePDF(rawContent: string, title = 'Red Whale Document'): Promise<string> {
  const doc = new jsPDF({ orientation: 'portrait', unit: 'mm', format: 'a4' });

  const PW = doc.internal.pageSize.getWidth();
  const PH = doc.internal.pageSize.getHeight();
  const M = 20;
  const CW = PW - M * 2;

  const content = cleanText(rawContent);
  const docTitle = cleanText(title).slice(0, 60);

  const RED_R = 185, RED_G = 28, RED_B = 28;
  const DARK_R = 31, DARK_G = 41, DARK_B = 55;
  const MUTED_R = 107, MUTED_G = 114, MUTED_B = 128;

  /* ═══════ COVER PAGE ═══════ */
  // Red top banner
  doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
  doc.rect(0, 0, PW, 60, 'F');
  doc.setFillColor(127, 29, 29);
  doc.rect(0, 58, PW, 2, 'F');

  // Decorative horizontal lines on right side of banner
  doc.setDrawColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.3);
  for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
    doc.line(PW - 55, 6 + i * 8, PW - 8, 6 + i * 8);
  }

  // Brand text
  doc.setTextColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(32);
  doc.text('RED WHALE', M, 32);

  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'italic');
  doc.setFontSize(12);
  doc.text('AI-Powered Intelligence', M, 42);

  // Decorative concentric circles on right
  doc.setDrawColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setLineWidth(1);
  doc.circle(PW - M - 16, 34, 11, 'S');
  doc.circle(PW - M - 16, 34, 6, 'S');
  doc.setFillColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.circle(PW - M - 16, 34, 2.5, 'F');

  // Document title block — use times for elegance
  let y = 78;
  doc.setTextColor(DARK_R, DARK_G, DARK_B);
  doc.setFont('times', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(24);
  const titleLines = doc.splitTextToSize(docTitle, CW);
  doc.text(titleLines, M, y);
  y += titleLines.length * 9 + 3;

  // Red accent underline
  doc.setDrawColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
  doc.setLineWidth(1.2);
  const tw = doc.getTextWidth(docTitle);
  doc.line(M, y, M + Math.min(tw, CW), y);
  y += 10;

  // Date
  doc.setTextColor(MUTED_R, MUTED_G, MUTED_B);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
  doc.setFontSize(11);
  doc.text(getDateStr(), M, y);
  y += 18;

  // Divider
  doc.setDrawColor(220, 220, 220);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.3);
  doc.line(M, y, PW - M, y);
  y += 12;

  // "Premium Document" badge
  doc.setFillColor(254, 242, 242);
  doc.roundedRect(M, y, 55, 10, 2, 2, 'F');
  doc.setTextColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(9);
  doc.text('Premium Document', M + 4, y + 6.5);

  /* ═══════ CONTENT PAGES ═══════ */
  const lines = content.split('\n');

  for (const raw of lines) {
    const line = raw.trim();
    if (!line) {
      y += 4;
      continue;
    }

    const words = line.split(/\s+/);
    const looksLikeHeading =
      line.length < 60 &&
      words.length <= 9 &&
      /^[A-Z0-9]/.test(line) &&
      !/\b(and|the|for|with|from|into|onto|upon|this|that|these|those|when|where|because|since|while|during|before|after|above|below|between|under|over|again|further|then|once|here|there|all|any|both|each|few|more|most|other|some|such|no|nor|not|only|own|same|so|than|too|very|can|will|just|should|now)\b/i.test(words[0] || '');

    const isBullet = isBulletLine(raw);
    const isNumbered = isNumberedLine(raw);

    const lineH = looksLikeHeading ? 5.5 : 4.8;
    const needed = looksLikeHeading ? 20 : isBullet || isNumbered ? 10 : 6;

    if (y + needed > PH - M - 10) {
      doc.addPage();
      // Light warm cream page fill
      doc.setFillColor(250, 250, 250);
      doc.rect(0, 0, PW, PH, 'F');
      // Top red accent line
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.rect(0, 0, PW, 1.5, 'F');
      // Left margin red accent
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.rect(0, 0, 1.5, PH, 'F');
      // Watermark
      doc.setTextColor(240, 240, 240);
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
      doc.setFontSize(48);
      doc.text('RED WHALE', PW / 2, PH / 2, { align: 'center', angle: 45 });
      y = M;
    }

    if (looksLikeHeading) {
      // Section card background
      doc.setFillColor(254, 242, 242);
      doc.roundedRect(M - 3, y - 7, CW + 6, 11, 1.5, 1.5, 'F');
      // Left red accent bar
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.rect(M - 3, y - 7, 2.5, 11, 'F');

      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
      doc.setFontSize(12);
      doc.setTextColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.text(line, M + 2, y);
      y += 14;
    } else if (isBullet) {
      // Red square bullet
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.rect(M, y - 2, 2.5, 2.5, 'F');

      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
      doc.setFontSize(10);
      doc.setTextColor(DARK_R, DARK_G, DARK_B);

      const body = line.replace(/^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/, '');
      const wrapped = doc.splitTextToSize(body, CW - 6);
      doc.text(wrapped, M + 6, y);
      y += wrapped.length * lineH + 3;
    } else if (isNumbered) {
      const match = line.match(/^\s*(\d+)\.\s+(.*)/);
      const num = match ? match[1] : '';
      const body = match ? match[2] : line;

      // Red number circle
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.circle(M + 3, y - 1, 3, 'F');
      doc.setTextColor(255, 255, 255);
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
      doc.setFontSize(7);
      doc.text(num, M + 3, y, { align: 'center' });

      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
      doc.setFontSize(10);
      doc.setTextColor(DARK_R, DARK_G, DARK_B);

      const wrapped = doc.splitTextToSize(body, CW - 10);
      doc.text(wrapped, M + 10, y);
      y += wrapped.length * lineH + 3;
    } else {
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
      doc.setFontSize(10);
      doc.setTextColor(DARK_R, DARK_G, DARK_B);

      const wrapped = doc.splitTextToSize(line, CW);
      doc.text(wrapped, M, y);
      y += wrapped.length * lineH + 2;
    }
  }

  /* ═══════ FOOTER (skip cover) ═══════ */
  const total = doc.getNumberOfPages();
  for (let p = 1; p <= total; p++) {
    doc.setPage(p);
    if (p === 1) continue;

    // Footer line
    doc.setDrawColor(210, 210, 210);
    doc.setLineWidth(0.2);
    doc.line(M, PH - 14, PW - M, PH - 14);

    // Footer text
    doc.setTextColor(MUTED_R, MUTED_G, MUTED_B);
    doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
    doc.setFontSize(8);
    doc.text('Generated by Red Whale V1', M, PH - 8);

    // Page number circle
    doc.setDrawColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
    doc.setLineWidth(0.3);
    doc.circle(PW - M - 5, PH - 9, 4, 'S');
    doc.setTextColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
    doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
    doc.setFontSize(7);
    doc.text(`${p - 1}`, PW - M - 5, PH - 8, { align: 'center' });
  }

  return doc.output('datauristring');
}

export function downloadPDF(dataUri: string, filename = 'red-whale-document.pdf'): void {
  const link = document.createElement('a');
  link.href = dataUri;
  link.download = filename;
  link.click();
}

```
// PDF Generator — Premium beautiful PDFs with Red Whale branding
import { jsPDF } from 'jspdf';

/* ─── helpers ─── */

const SAFE_REGEX = /[^\u0020-\u007E\u0900-\u097F\u00B0\u00BD\u00A0\n\r\t]/g;

/** Collapse spaced single-letter words: "M U S T" → "MUST" while keeping other tokens intact */
function collapseSpacedLetters(line: string): string {
  const trimmed = line.trim();
  const tokens = trimmed.split(/\s+/);
  if (tokens.length < 3) return line;

  const singleLetters = tokens.filter((t) => /^[A-Za-z]$/.test(t)).length;
  if (singleLetters / tokens.length <= 0.4) return line;

  const out: string[] = [];
  let run: string[] = [];
  const flush = () => {
    if (run.length) { out.push(run.join('')); run = []; }
  };
  for (const tok of tokens) {
    if (/^[A-Za-z]$/.test(tok)) {
      run.push(tok);
    } else {
      flush();
      out.push(tok);
    }
  }
  flush();
  return out.join(' ');
}

function cleanText(text: string): string {
  let t = text;
  t = t.replace(/```[\s\S]*?```/g, '');
  t = t.replace(/`([^`]*)`/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/\*\*([^*]+)\*\*/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/\*([^*]+)\*/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/__([^_]+)__/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/_([^_]+)_/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/^#{1,6}\s+/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\([^)]+\)/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\[[^\]]*\]/g, '$1');
  t = t.replace(/https?:\/\/[^\s]+/g, '');
  t = t.replace(/\|/g, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*[-:]+[-\s:]*\s*$/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(SAFE_REGEX, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*=?\d+\s*/gm, '');
  t = t.replace(/^\s*[<>=]+\s*/gm, '');
  t = t.split('\n').map(collapseSpacedLetters).join('\n');
  t = t.replace(/[ \t]+/g, ' ');
  t = t.replace(/\n{3,}/g, '\n\n');
  return t.trim();
}

function getDateStr(): string {
  const d = new Date();
  return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' });
}

function isBulletLine(line: string): boolean {
  return /^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/.test(line);
}

function isNumberedLine(line: string): boolean {
  return /^\s*\d+\.\s+/.test(line);
}

function isAllCapsOrTitleCase(line: string): boolean {
  const words = line.split(/\s+/).filter(Boolean);
  if (words.length === 0) return false;
  const allUpper = words.every((w) => /^[A-Z0-9]+$/.test(w));
  if (allUpper) return true;
  const titleCase = words.every((w) => /^[A-Z0-9]/.test(w));
  return titleCase;
}

/* ─── detect whether a PDF button should show ─── */
export function isStructuredContent(text: string): boolean {
  const hasTable = /\|.+/m.test(text);
  const hasSchedule = /\b(monday|tuesday|wednesday|thursday|friday|saturday|sunday|time|schedule|timetable|routine|plan|report|summary|table|chart|list|ingredient|step|material|recipe|steps|ingredients)\b/i.test(text);
  const hasHeadings = /^#{1,6}\s+/m.test(text);
  const hasLists = /^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/m.test(text);
  return hasTable || (hasSchedule && (hasHeadings || hasLists));
}

/* ─── main PDF builder ─── */
export async function generatePDF(rawContent: string, title = 'Red Whale Document'): Promise<string> {
  const doc = new jsPDF({ orientation: 'portrait', unit: 'mm', format: 'a4' });

  const PW = doc.internal.pageSize.getWidth();
  const PH = doc.internal.pageSize.getHeight();
  const M = 20;
  const CW = PW - M * 2;

  const content = cleanText(rawContent);
  const docTitle = cleanText(title).slice(0, 60);

  const RED_R = 185, RED_G = 28, RED_B = 28;
  const DARK_R = 31, DARK_G = 41, DARK_B = 55;
  const MUTED_R = 107, MUTED_G = 114, MUTED_B = 128;

  /* ═══════ COVER PAGE ═══════ */
  doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
  doc.rect(0, 0, PW, 60, 'F');
  doc.setFillColor(127, 29, 29);
  doc.rect(0, 58, PW, 2, 'F');

  doc.setDrawColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.3);
  for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
    doc.line(PW - 55, 6 + i * 8, PW - 8, 6 + i * 8);
  }

  doc.setTextColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(32);
  doc.text('RED WHALE', M, 32);

  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'italic');
  doc.setFontSize(12);
  doc.text('AI-Powered Intelligence', M, 42);

  doc.setDrawColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.setLineWidth(1);
  doc.circle(PW - M - 16, 34, 11, 'S');
  doc.circle(PW - M - 16, 34, 6, 'S');
  doc.setFillColor(255, 255, 255);
  doc.circle(PW - M - 16, 34, 2.5, 'F');

  let y = 78;
  doc.setTextColor(DARK_R, DARK_G, DARK_B);
  doc.setFont('times', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(24);
  const titleLines = doc.splitTextToSize(docTitle, CW);
  doc.text(titleLines, M, y);
  y += titleLines.length * 9 + 3;

  doc.setDrawColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
  doc.setLineWidth(1.2);
  const tw = doc.getTextWidth(docTitle);
  doc.line(M, y, M + Math.min(tw, CW), y);
  y += 10;

  doc.setTextColor(MUTED_R, MUTED_G, MUTED_B);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
  doc.setFontSize(11);
  doc.text(getDateStr(), M, y);
  y += 18;

  doc.setDrawColor(220, 220, 220);
  doc.setLineWidth(0.3);
  doc.line(M, y, PW - M, y);
  y += 12;

  doc.setFillColor(254, 242, 242);
  doc.roundedRect(M, y, 55, 10, 2, 2, 'F');
  doc.setTextColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
  doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
  doc.setFontSize(9);
  doc.text('Premium Document', M + 4, y + 6.5);

  /* ═══════ CONTENT PAGES ═══════ */
  const lines = content.split('\n');

  for (const raw of lines) {
    const line = raw.trim();
    if (!line) {
      y += 5;
      continue;
    }

    const words = line.split(/\s+/);
    // STRICT heading detection: short, few words, ALL words capitalized, no common words
    const looksLikeHeading =
      line.length < 40 &&
      words.length >= 2 &&
      words.length <= 6 &&
      isAllCapsOrTitleCase(line) &&
      !/\b(and|the|for|with|from|into|onto|upon|this|that|these|those|when|where|because|since|while|during|before|after|above|below|between|under|over|again|further|then|once|here|there|all|any|both|each|few|more|most|other|some|such|no|nor|not|only|own|same|so|than|too|very|can|will|just|should|now)\b/i.test(words[0] || '');

    const isBullet = isBulletLine(raw);
    const isNumbered = isNumberedLine(raw);

    // Pick font & size BEFORE calculating height
    let font = 'helvetica';
    let style: 'normal' | 'bold' = 'normal';
    let size = 10;
    let textColorR = DARK_R, textColorG = DARK_G, textColorB = DARK_B;
    let indent = 0;
    let extraPad = 0;

    if (looksLikeHeading) {
      font = 'helvetica'; style = 'bold'; size = 12;
      textColorR = RED_R; textColorG = RED_G; textColorB = RED_B;
      extraPad = 6;
    } else if (isBullet) {
      font = 'helvetica'; style = 'normal'; size = 10;
      indent = 6; extraPad = 3;
    } else if (isNumbered) {
      font = 'helvetica'; style = 'normal'; size = 10;
      indent = 10; extraPad = 3;
    }

    doc.setFont(font, style);
    doc.setFontSize(size);

    const body = isBullet ? line.replace(/^\s*[\-\*•]\s+/, '')
      : isNumbered ? (line.match(/^\s*\d+\.\s+(.*)/)?.[2] ?? line)
      : line;

    const wrapped = doc.splitTextToSize(body, CW - indent);
    const lineH = size * 0.5; // fontSize * 0.5 ≈ mm per line
    const textH = wrapped.length * lineH;
    const needed = textH + extraPad + 4;

    // Page break before rendering
    if (y + needed > PH - M - 10) {
      doc.addPage();
      doc.setFillColor(250, 250, 250);
      doc.rect(0, 0, PW, PH, 'F');
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.rect(0, 0, PW, 1.5, 'F');
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.rect(0, 0, 1.5, PH, 'F');
      // Watermark
      doc.setTextColor(240, 240, 240);
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
      doc.setFontSize(48);
      doc.text('RED WHALE', PW / 2, PH / 2, { align: 'center', angle: 45 });
      y = M;
    }

    if (looksLikeHeading) {
      // Section card
      doc.setFillColor(254, 242, 242);
      doc.roundedRect(M - 3, y - 7, CW + 6, 11, 1.5, 1.5, 'F');
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.rect(M - 3, y - 7, 2.5, 11, 'F');
      doc.setTextColor(textColorR, textColorG, textColorB);
      doc.text(wrapped, M + 2, y);
      y += textH + extraPad + 4;
    } else if (isBullet) {
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.rect(M, y - 2, 2.5, 2.5, 'F');
      doc.setTextColor(textColorR, textColorG, textColorB);
      doc.text(wrapped, M + indent, y);
      y += textH + extraPad + 2;
    } else if (isNumbered) {
      const match = line.match(/^\s*(\d+)\.\s+(.*)/);
      const num = match ? match[1] : '';
      doc.setFillColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
      doc.circle(M + 3, y - 1, 3, 'F');
      doc.setTextColor(255, 255, 255);
      doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
      doc.setFontSize(7);
      doc.text(num, M + 3, y, { align: 'center' });
      doc.setFont(font, style);
      doc.setFontSize(size);
      doc.setTextColor(textColorR, textColorG, textColorB);
      doc.text(wrapped, M + indent, y);
      y += textH + extraPad + 2;
    } else {
      doc.setTextColor(textColorR, textColorG, textColorB);
      doc.text(wrapped, M, y);
      y += textH + 4;
    }
  }

  /* ═══════ FOOTER (skip cover) ═══════ */
  const total = doc.getNumberOfPages();
  for (let p = 1; p <= total; p++) {
    doc.setPage(p);
    if (p === 1) continue;

    doc.setDrawColor(210, 210, 210);
    doc.setLineWidth(0.2);
    doc.line(M, PH - 14, PW - M, PH - 14);

    doc.setTextColor(MUTED_R, MUTED_G, MUTED_B);
    doc.setFont('helvetica', 'normal');
    doc.setFontSize(8);
    doc.text('Generated by Red Whale V2', M, PH - 8);

    doc.setDrawColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
    doc.setLineWidth(0.3);
    doc.circle(PW - M - 5, PH - 9, 4, 'S');
    doc.setTextColor(RED_R, RED_G, RED_B);
    doc.setFont('helvetica', 'bold');
    doc.setFontSize(7);
    doc.text(`${p - 1}`, PW - M - 5, PH - 8, { align: 'center' });
  }

  return doc.output('datauristring');
}

export function downloadPDF(dataUri: string, filename = 'red-whale-document.pdf'): void {
  const link = document.createElement('a');
  link.href = dataUri;
  link.download = filename;
  link.click();
}
